Tian Songyao's Telegram to Zhang Qun 30

(Nanjing) Tian Songyao's telegram to Zhang Qun regarding the method of eliminating the Sichuan war stated: "Your esteemed telegram has been respectfully received. I deeply admire your brother's painstaking efforts to eliminate the scourge of war and stabilize the homeland in Sichuan. I also strongly advocate that Sichuan affairs be resolved through political methods. Your brother's proposal to reorganize Sichuan politics, based on the Central Government's mandate and adopting public opinion in Sichuan, establishing a committee with representatives from the gentry and people to openly discuss implementation measures, to resolve disputes and open up a new situation, is something I greatly admire and endorse. I am now proclaiming this to the public and friendly armies, hoping that you, brother, will exert great efforts to realize it as soon as possible. However, I would like to add that with the national crisis at hand, internal strife is constantly occurring. No person of insight does not feel pained by this. The Central Government and the people of the country unanimously avoid mentioning civil war, but they do not know that if the root of civil war is not removed, the outbreak of civil war is inevitable. If they avoid treatment and only know how to perfunctorily mediate, not only will they lose prestige, but they may also be unable to quell the scourge. For the sake of the Central Government, they should clearly distinguish right from wrong to determine justice. Anyone who raises troops and causes trouble, and is not supported by public opinion and is difficult to condone in principle, should be ordered to be sanctioned once it is verified. If they refuse to submit to sanctions, they should be explicitly ordered to be suppressed. Rewards should come from utmost impartiality, and likes and dislikes should be shared with the people, so that the fundamental principles can be revitalized and civil war can be eliminated. This is not only for the sake of Sichuan affairs. However, the dispute in Sichuan has been going on for more than two months. The Central Government cannot but understand the rights and wrongs of the matter and the direction of the people's hearts. Therefore, the Central Government should quickly deal with it to relieve the suffering of the people and alleviate the worries in the west, and should not sit and listen to the evolution of the situation. I hope that you will report this to the Central Government, and I especially hope that my brother will exert great efforts. Sincerely replying, please forgive my ignorance. Your younger brother, Tian Songyao, bows." (Special dispatch from the 12th)

British Government's Note to the U.S. on War Debts Expires, Payment Still Made 57

However, declaration made that it cannot be regarded as a recurrence of the repayment system; further negotiations are necessary before next June. ▲ London, 11th (Reuters) – Today, the British government issued a note to the U.S. State Department stating that the December 15th debt installment will be paid in gold. This is because, under the current circumstances, it is the least burdensome method for the British government. It was then clearly stated that this payment must be regarded as the last batch under the existing Anglo-American war debt agreement and cannot be seen as the beginning of a renewed payment of the amounts stipulated in that agreement. This payment is only being made because time is too short for further discussion. Moreover, the U.S.'s insistence on this payment greatly increases the hope of re-examining the entire war debt structure. Therefore, it is specifically declared that the amount paid this time must be regarded as part of the final settlement amount in the future. It also emphasized the importance of both countries exchanging views on the war debt issue as soon as possible, urging negotiations on this matter before June 15th next year to avoid the risk of total destruction of current international agreements. Britain still firmly believes that there is no other way to reduce the danger of exchange rate fluctuations other than postponing the payment due on November 15th. Therefore, it deeply regrets the U.S.'s decision to collect the debt. It further declared that Britain firmly believes that resuming war debt payments would inevitably lead to economic disasters; therefore, the current payment must not be regarded as a return to normal debt repayment.

U.S. Reply Rejects British Conditions for Payment 58

▲ Washington, 11th (Havas) – The U.S. response, after being reviewed by Hoover over the phone, was delivered to British Ambassador Sir Ronald Lindsay. The reply noted that the U.S. government was willing to put on record the British government's decision to pay the installment due on December 15th. However, regarding the reservations in the British note, the reply stated: "The U.S. Treasury Secretary cannot accept payment except according to the conditions contained in the agreement for settling war debts." It also stated, "Only the U.S. Congress has the power to change the obligations assumed by each government." The reply further stated that the U.S. State Department considered that "the measures the British government intends to propose after a comprehensive study of the war debt issue in the future, as mentioned in the fifth and sixth paragraphs of its note, are merely an opinion." Regarding this point, the reply reiterated the U.S. note of December 8th, stating that President Hoover was prepared to study the entire war debt issue and propose various plans to stabilize exchange rates, restore commerce, and raise prices. However, the reply declared that the U.S. government and people attached great importance to maintaining the current war debt agreement; therefore, the U.S. rejected Britain's reservation regarding the December 15th war debt installment. Although very polite, it firmly opposed it. The drafting of the U.S. reply was extremely swift; the State Department delivered the reply to the British Ambassador six hours after receiving the British note. According to observations from well-informed sources, the reiteration of the current war debt agreement in the reply was a method used by the U.S. government to avoid attacks from within the country. It is well known that the U.S. government actually wanted to agree with Britain's statement, but it is also a fact that the U.S. Congress has supreme power over this matter. The U.S. State Department believes that the French note will also contain a statement similar to the British note, and the U.S. reply will be the same as the reply to Britain.

France's Attitude Consistent with Britain; Herriot Explains War Debt Case to Parliament 59

▲ Paris, 10th (Reuters) – The French cabinet decided to pay the U.S. debt installment due on December 15th, but with reservations, to act in concert with Britain. The Finance Committee and the Foreign Affairs Committee of the Chamber of Deputies also advocated payment. Therefore, the debate in Parliament tomorrow is no longer of concern to the public. However, everything still depends on the nature of the reservations. Currently, the right-wing party is entirely against payment, the central party's attitude is unclear, the Radical Party mostly advocates payment, and the Socialist Party, which holds the overall view, is very indifferent. If Herriot treats this as a matter of confidence, then the fate of the cabinet may depend on the number of votes in favor or against. If he does not treat this as a matter of confidence, then the chance of parliamentarians supporting payment, even with reservations, will decrease.

▲ Paris, 11th (Havas) – Unless something unexpected happens, the Chamber of Deputies will discuss the war debt issue on Monday according to the following procedure: Premier Herriot will take the stage at 3 p.m. to deliver a declaration in the name of the government, providing a comprehensive explanation of the war debt issue, and report to the Chamber of Deputies the reasons for the government's decision regarding the debt installment due on the 15th of this month. Normally, after a cabinet declaration, parliamentarians would immediately stand up to respond. This time, only one person will be allowed to respond after Herriot's speech. Subsequently, the government will request the parliament to immediately discuss the war debt case. At this point, the speaker will announce a recess for at least one hour to allow the government's proposal to be posted. If there are draft laws, amendments from various committees, or counter-proposals, they will be posted at the same time as the government proposal. During the recess, the Foreign Affairs and Finance Committees will discuss the government proposal. If there are any doubts that Premier Herriot needs to explain, the Premier can also attend and respond. After the committees' discussion, the formal large-scale debate on various proposals in the Chamber of Deputies will begin. The registered parliamentarians will raise questions to the government. The full text of the cabinet proposal will only be finalized tomorrow. In short, regardless of the procedures, the cabinet will submit a draft law to the Chamber of Deputies requesting the disbursement of funds to repay the $96,000,000 due on the war debt. If this case is approved by the Chamber of Deputies, the government will then attend the Senate to explain everything.

German Military Reduction Policy Successful; Equal Rights Achieved 61

Detailed discussions may face obstacles

Germany still reserves the freedom to withdraw

Five-Power Declaration delivered to the Chairman of the Disarmament Conference

Key members to meet soon in Geneva

▲ Berlin, 11th (Reuters) – The German people regard the German arms equality plan set in Geneva as a great victory for German disarmament policy. There were frequent telephone calls between Berlin and Geneva last night and this morning. German Foreign Minister Neurath spoke with German Chancellor Schleicher several times for a considerable amount of time. Schleicher then went to meet President Hindenburg. Afterwards, he instructed the Foreign Minister to formally sign the agreement. German officials believe that this plan is equivalent to stipulating that all provisions of Chapter 5 of the Treaty of Versailles, if they can be equally applied to all countries participating in the Disarmament Conference, are effective. Germany also believes that if the principle of equality is denied in the details, Germany still has the freedom to withdraw from the Disarmament Conference. If obstacles arise in the implementation of this principle in the future, Germany can be in a dominant position, because it can point out to the world that this agreement is not being observed.

▲ Geneva, 11th (Reuters) – The declaration signed by British Prime Minister MacDonald, U.S. Representative Norman Davis, French Representative Paul-Boncour, German Foreign Minister Neurath, and Italian Representative Aloisi, granting Germany equal rights to participate in the Disarmament Conference, has been delivered to the Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, today. The declaration contains the intention to include various restrictions on the arms of all countries in the future Disarmament Convention, and clarifies that the implementation of these equal rights will be discussed at the conference. The principle of equality must be included in the Disarmament Convention.

▲ Geneva, 11th (Reuters) – British Prime Minister MacDonald is departing for London tonight. Although he feels tired, he will still stop in Paris for several hours. Key members of the Disarmament Conference are scheduled to meet within this week, but the Disarmament Conference will be postponed until January. The new step being planned is for the Five Powers to meet in London on January 15th. The Chairman of the Disarmament Conference, Henderson, will also attend this and subsequent Five-Power meetings. U.S. Representative Norman Davis is scheduled to depart for New York on Tuesday. His plan to include various measures already agreed upon by the Disarmament Conference in a convention will likely be discussed at the London meeting in January. British Foreign Secretary Simon will remain in Geneva until the end of this week due to the Sino-Japanese incident. There is reason to believe that the work of the Special Committee of Nineteen cannot proceed smoothly, and the explicit topic of non-recognition of "Manchukuo" will soon be brought up for discussion.

Japanese Armored Vehicles Fiercely Bomb Shanhaiguan 64

Destroying Our Agencies and Civilian Homes While Falsely Accusing Us of Firing First

Rumors Spread of Simultaneous Uprisings in Tianjin, Peiping, and Yuguan on the 15th

Intended to Support Japanese Army's Attack on Rehe, But We Are Fully Prepared

Tianjin Correspondent – The Japanese army is pressing the Northeastern Anti-Japanese Volunteer Army with seven divisions of troops. General Su Bingwen fought bitterly at Haiman for two months, annihilating more than 20,000 Japanese rebels. Later, due to limited ammunition reserves and no way to replenish them, he reluctantly and tearfully announced on the 4th of this month that he was retreating into Russian territory. Now that the military situation in Northern Manchuria has come to an end, the Japanese army is shifting its aggressive gaze to Rehe. Their plan is to station one division on the Haiman line, one division on the Harbin-Changchun line, and one division to suppress the Volunteer Army of Ding Chao and Li Du. The remaining four divisions, after a short rest and replenishment, will take the South Manchuria Railway and enter the puppet Fengshan Road, stationing troops in Jinzhou, Yixian, Zhangwu, and Tongliao, and attacking Rehe in three routes. Another route will seize Shanhaiguan. This is the first step in their military plan. Once Rehe and Yuguan are captured, they will advance towards Peiping and Tianjin. This is the second step. Once Peiping and Tianjin are captured, they will advance along the Peiping-Hankou, Peiping-Suiyuan, and Tianjin-Pukou Railways, and move the puppet regime into the old capital. This is the third step. However, Rehe is covered with mountains and difficult to attack. Tanks are useless, and artillery and aircraft are not very effective. Therefore, the Japanese had long planned to use political means to acquire Rehe. Unexpectedly, Tang Yulin's attitude was unpredictable. So they changed their methods and spent huge sums of money to buy out traitors, who sneaked into the border of Rehe, propagated resistance against Japan and expulsion of Tang, guided the armed masses, and organized a puppet self-defense force. Originally, the folk customs of Rehe were simple and honest, and they had suffered too much from the pain of harsh government in recent years. As long as someone led the expulsion of Tang, they would follow like the wind, without considering that they were working for the Japanese.

In view of the above, Rehe, Peiping, Tianjin, and Yuguan have entered a troubled autumn. On the afternoon of the 8th of this month, the Japanese army sent armored trains from Suizhong to make provocative moves outside Shanhaiguan. The Japanese garrison stationed in Yuguan also sent out armed sentries to move around, and the situation was extremely tense. At 10 p.m., the Japanese armored train fired more than a dozen shells into the city at the east entrance of Shanhaiguan Railway Station. He Guozhu, commander of our 9th Brigade, immediately sent personnel to negotiate, but to no avail. The armored train even rushed into the pass and fired 20 to 30 shells between Qinhuangdao and Shihezi, destroying the railway station's water pump (i.e., the water tower on the locomotives) and injuring a guard. At 11 p.m., it returned to Shanhaiguan, hooked our army's telecommunications train to the armored train, dragged it out of the pass, dismantled our radio station equipment, and transported it away. At this time, the military's morale was indignant and the public's morale was panic-stricken. Commander He immediately reported to Zhang Xueliang via long-distance telephone and asked for instructions. Zhang immediately ordered "peaceful handling, no rash action." He immediately followed the instructions and strictly instructed his subordinates to remain calm. Therefore, the sub-customs of Qinhuangdao Customs, established in Yuguan, was attacked by thugs directed by Japanese soldiers, who robbed the tax money and the Japanese goods detained for tax evasion. At the same time, they used hand grenades to attack the Public Security Bureau and robbed the bayonets and firearms. At 2 a.m. on the 9th, the armored train rushed into the pass again and traveled between Qinhuangdao and Shanhaiguan, blocking the tracks with obstacles. Therefore, the eastbound trains on the Beining Railway only reached Qinhuangdao. After repeated negotiations with the Railway Bureau, and since many refugees had gathered at Yuguan Railway Station and had to be transported, the Japanese army finally agreed to remove the obstacles. The Railway Bureau prepared more than a dozen third-class carriages to transport refugees to Qinhuangdao, who then took trains west. Commander He, accompanied by Public Security Bureau Chief Mao, went to the headquarters of the Japanese garrison in the morning of the 9th to negotiate. Unexpectedly, the commander, Wakaho, took out a written document stating that Chinese troops had first fired at the Japanese armored train, and the Japanese army had returned fire in self-defense, etc., and forced He to sign it. At this time, the armored train fired six or seven more shells as a demonstration. He refused to sign because it violated the facts. Wakaho knew that he could not force him, so he changed his tune and said that he would reinvestigate and talk again at 3 p.m. At the appointed time, Commander He went to the Japanese garrison, but Wakaho said that according to the investigation report, there were many Volunteer Army troops hidden inside and outside Yuguan City, and there was gunfire in the city last night, so they fired shells. However, he did not admit to towing away our army's telecommunications train, dismantling the radio station, robbing our customs, and attacking our Public Security Bureau, resulting in no results. After the incident, an investigation revealed that three shells fell on the sub-customs, injuring three customs officers. One shell fell in front of the county education bureau, shattering the mounting stone in front of the door. Two shells fell in the 9th Brigade headquarters and the Public Security Bureau, but did not explode. One shell fell on each of the following: Juhua Hall, Juhua Inn, Qianfuxin Pharmacy, Fan's small shop, Zhao's bun shop, He's residence on North Street, and the 5th Elementary School, all of which exploded and destroyed the houses. One shell fell on Wang's vegetable garden at Jiaolouwan, but did not explode. Two shells fell on the empty land west of Shuixi, one shell fell on Wang's tomb, two shells fell on the Xiaolingguan Temple, and one shell fell on the west entrance of Shuncheng Street. The total number of shells was 23. There were still 20 to 30 other shells that had not yet been found. The people of Yuguan had all dug cellars, and when they heard the sound of shelling, they fled into the cellars, so there were no casualties. Also, at 9 a.m. and 12 p.m. on the 9th, a Japanese aircraft flew from Qian'an to Yuguan for low-altitude reconnaissance. The east and south gates of Lin'yu County were tightly closed, while the north and west gates were open. The city market was in a state of semi-shutdown, fully demonstrating a bleak and terrifying scene. All schools were closed and the students scattered. The Japanese army dug trenches at Nadaotai's tomb, more than ten miles east of the east gate. Commander He also deployed defensive works at Erlidianzi, two miles outside the east gate, and transferred the 665th Regiment from the county to reinforce the defense. According to Shanhaiguan long-distance telephone reports, although last night (9th) passed peacefully, the Japanese armored train did not retreat, and the Japanese aircraft came again this morning, causing unrest and mass evacuation. The Japanese army is building a large airfield at Xujiawopu, east of the Nanling station on the Jin-Chao branch line, forcing 3,000 to 4,000 laborers to work hard, and building a highway from Beipiao through Nanling to Rehe.

Lieutenant Colonel Nakamura Kotaro, commander of the Japanese army stationed in Tianjin, sent Staff Officer Miura to Yuguan yesterday (9th) noon to exchange military opinions. He also sent more than 300 artillerymen to Yuguan to prepare for battle, and dispatched the destroyer Asagao from Dalian to Tianjin to await orders. Japanese Consul Sangishima in Tianjin visited Provincial Chairman Yu Xuezhong at 2 p.m. yesterday, stating that the Chinese troops in Yuguan were provoking the Japanese army and requesting that they be stopped immediately. The Japanese embassy in Peiping also made similar protests to Zhang Xueliang. Yu Xuezhong sent personnel to Yuguan last night to investigate everything. It is now rumored that the Japanese army will launch an attack in Peiping, Tianjin, and Yuguan on the 15th of this month to support the Japanese army's attack on Rehe. According to our authorities, this information may be a bluff and may not be reliable, but our side is adequately prepared. If they really come to make trouble, we have a responsibility to defend our territory and will not give up. The power of the Japanese army lies in tanks and aircraft. If there is street fighting, both sides are equal. Therefore, this time our side has not prepared sandbags and electric fences, because in street fighting, if soldiers hide behind electric fences and sandbags, they will not want to move forward. If there are no electric fences and sandbags to rely on, they must quickly move forward and fight when they see the enemy attacking. Our northern warriors must at least make the Japanese army have a proper understanding. (December 10th)

Jinan National Music Concert 65

The Chu Se and Qin Qiut presented without any vulgarity

High mountains and flowing water should have discerning listeners

Jinan Correspondent – The National Music Concert of the Datong Music Association was held at the People's Cinema at 4 p.m. today (10th). More than 400 people attended. It opened on time. The first thing that entered the audience's ears and eyes was the "National Music Suite, Chapter 3" played by all the members of the association. Then Wang Bingnan performed a solo on the ancient se "Shouyang Palace". The sound was melodious and the entire audience was silent. Before long, the sound subsided and the curtain fell. After a brief arrangement, Tian Yinghui's ancient qin solo appeared. The name of the song was "Drunken Fisherman Singing in the Evening", playing leisurely, intermittently, as if a drunken fisherman were beating his boat on the Jiangtan beach and singing folk songs. Then, as applause sounded, Yang Shao Yi's pipa solo "Spring River Flower Moon Night" began to play, sometimes tight, sometimes relaxed, like a complaint, like a plea, melodious and pleasant. Following Yang was Wang Dianyu's silk string performance. The program was "Weaving Room Teaching Son", with vivid imitations of trumpets, sheng pipes, military bands, etc., leaving the listeners amazed. Next was the "Guo Jie Lou" ensemble by the Jinpu Railway National Music Troupe. More than a dozen people participated, the sound stopping the clouds, and the aftersound circling the beams, making the atmosphere in the hall tense. Soon, Li Huaxuan's erhu solo "Liu Qing Niang" appeared, performing a song in which he changed his tune seven times, the sound of the oriole was clear and pleasant, and graceful and pleasing. Next was Yang Sheng Yi and Wang Bingnan's duet on pipa and other instruments, "Moon High". Song Binglan, a female, sang the Kunqu opera "Bu Bu Jiao" and "Ma Zai Bo". Fu Jingyuan's erhu solo "Autumn Wind Falling Leaves" was desolate and sad, touching the audience. The finale was the entire ensemble of "Qiu Ying Qu". It ended at six o'clock. (December 10th)

Another Drug Manufacturing Facility Discovered in Guoyang

Bengbu Correspondent – After Chen Zaigong, the main criminal in the Mengcheng heroin manufacturing case in northern Anhui, was captured and escorted to Bengbu, the principal offender, Li Mingxun, and more than 20 accomplices, including Yu Yiting, Li Xiuqing, and Wang Ziqing, all fled upon hearing the news, and the drug manufacturing equipment was also secretly hidden. He immediately led the Third Squadron of the Public Security Bureau to investigate and, sure enough, discovered it on the spot, seizing more than 200 taels of heroin, a large batch of opium, a drug manufacturing machine, and more than 20 barrels of gasoline, and arresting six criminals involved in manufacturing drugs: Wang Hanqing, Lu Zhongyang, Li Wen, Jin Yunlu, He Chungao, and Yang Ru, and escorting them to the county. Xu immediately interrogated them personally, and the criminals confessed to manufacturing drugs without reservation. Xu immediately telegraphed the province for instructions, and the provincial government replied, ordering that the criminals be sentenced to three or five years of imprisonment and fined between one and ten thousand yuan. Xu has complied with the telegram. Mengcheng and Guoyang counties are adjacent, and the manufacturing of drugs is well known in the vicinity. With these successive crackdowns, the drug atmosphere in northern Anhui may be slightly curbed. (December 10th)

Jiangsu Province Land Deed Tax Reduced for One Month 67

From the 20th of this month to the 20th of February

During this period, both the basic and surtaxes will be collected at half price

On the 9th of this month, the Jiangsu Provincial Government Committee passed the Finance Department's proposal at its 550th meeting: The land deed tax in this province has not been actively paid due to the low grain prices and economic depression this year. From the 20th of this December to the 20th of next January, it will be collected at half of the original tax rate. During this one-month price reduction period, the original surtaxes and capital donations will also be collected at half price uniformly, and the stipulated overdue penalties will also be waived to reduce the burden on the people. The original proposal of the Finance Department is recorded as follows: "The land deed tax in this province is designated as the construction public bond fund. Currently, due to the low grain prices and economic depression this year, the land deed tax in various counties has not been actively paid, and the fifth issuance period is approaching. It is estimated that the fund for principal and interest repayment is very far short, and we must quickly find relief methods. The land deed tax rate was originally set at nine and six for sales and mortgages. To promote the vigorous collection of land deed tax, it is necessary to have a special price reduction to attract business. It is proposed that from the 20th of this December to the 20th of January, we will collect half of the original tax rate for one month. During this one-month price reduction period, the original surtaxes and capital donations will also be collected at half price uniformly, and the stipulated overdue penalties will also be waived to reduce the burden on the people and promote the vigorous collection of land deed tax. Is this appropriate for the sake of consolidating the credit of the public bond fund? Please decide publicly."

The Suzhou High Court Sentences Hu Lifu to Life Imprisonment 68

Suzhou Dispatch: (Today, the 12th) was the day for sentencing the traitor Hu Li. Mistaking a Pirate Ship, Temporary Martial Law 79

A Hong Porcelain boat in Zhapu sailed out to sea the day before yesterday and suddenly saw a pirate ship approaching. The boat deliberately dodged east and west, but the pirate ship kept chasing it, so it repeatedly fled into the estuary, hurriedly landed, reported to the fishing protection team, and transferred the information to the Public Security Bureau, the Tax Police Team, and the Security Corps. However, the pirate ship had already chased and sailed into the entrance. All the teams rushed to the seawall to guard it. As expected, the pirate ship sailed in with its sails raised, and they fired guns and shouted to stop it, firing more than twenty shots in total. At the same time, the city announced temporary martial law. Seeing bullets raining down, the sailing boat hung a mast light, obeyed the order to drop anchor, and sent a representative on a small boat, claiming to be a hemp skin boat from Shaoxing, which had also encountered pirates in the middle of the journey but had escaped by speeding up. The Public Security Bureau then telegraphed the Shaoxing Customs Brokerage, which replied that it was indeed a law-abiding merchant, and the sailing boat was released on bail yesterday.

Shaoxing

Pirates Rob Ships Outside the Dongjiang Estuary 80

Yao Wen[Blank]'s large ship, from Zhentangdian, Shaoxing, was hired by Shen Xiangxing's Guotang Firm in Xinbutou to load eight hundred and dozens jars of Shaoxing wine and six thousand one hundred and dozens empty jars. When it sailed outside the Dongjiang Estuary, a pirate ship suddenly appeared. More than twenty pirates, each holding a wooden shell gun, completely robbed the ship and its cargo. Six sailors were only allowed to return one to inform the shipowner to prepare funds for redemption.

Bengbu

Bandits Rampant at the Border of Anhui and Henan 81

Futi is located in the northwest of Anhui, bordering Henan to the west, and has always been an area where bandits emerge. The area has been severely affected by banditry for many years. Although government troops and local militias have made efforts to suppress them, they have not been able to completely eliminate them. Recently, with the approach of winter and the end of the year, many hungry people have taken risks and joined the bandits, gathering at night, and gradually forming bandit gangs. The bandit leaders Zhao Hongshan, Zhang Siyan, Yang Xiaoheizi, and others, with more than 400 bandits, have recently gathered in the Li Gang Bridge area, more than 20 li from the Zhaiji, in the tenth district of Futi, entrenched and harassing, only 180 li from the county seat. They are burning, killing, raping, and looting, and the situation is extremely rampant. Residents are fleeing. In recent days, they have gathered more and more, and their momentum has become increasingly large. They have also fled to the Guan Yuemiao Zhangjiawa area on the border of Anhui and Henan. The county government of the neighboring county has telegraphed the Fourth Division Commander Xu Tingyao, stationed in Bengbu, to send troops to suppress them.

The Beginning and End of the Chengdu Street Fighting 82

The Origin of the Sichuan War – The Special Situation of Chengdu

The Course of the Street Fighting – The Human Hell After the War

This Sichuan war is like a sore on a person's body, which has been accumulating for five or six years, and it cannot but fester. Sichuan Province has a large area, many mountains, and inconvenient transportation, so it is easy to produce feudal warlords. Since Yang Sen's defeat, four big bosses have remained: one in Chongqing, commonly known as Yu Liu (i.e., Liu Xiang), the commander of the Twenty-first Army; and three in Chengdu: one is Liu Wenhui, the commander of the Twenty-fourth Army, who is also the chairman of the provincial government, commonly known as Provincial Liu; one is Deng Xihou, the commander of the Twenty-eighth Army; and one is Tian Songyao, the commander of the Twenty-ninth Army, collectively known as the Deng Tian Liu Three Army Commanders.

Generally speaking, the Second Liu's forces are the largest. One occupies Chongqing, controlling more than 20 counties in eastern Sichuan, with its military strength extending to Shashi in Hubei, and its tax revenue is extremely strong. The other occupies Chengdu, with its subordinate counties accounting for half of Sichuan (more than 70 counties), and rich areas such as Yongchuan, Neijiang, Zizhong, and Ziyang are all within it, and its tax revenue is also good. The former (Liu Xiang) holds the title of Director-General of Sichuan Rehabilitation and has extraordinary ambitions, with the idea of unifying Sichuan and becoming the leader of the Southwest, so he spares no effort in preparing his troops and horses. Now, the Sichuan River has his warships, and Yuxian has his airfield. He is the commander of the army, navy, and air force, and his power is more and more oppressive. Provincial Liu inevitably has many things that he cannot get away with. The most obvious is the withholding of all military supplies he purchased downstream, and after a long time, even the medical supplies are withheld. Provincial Liu did not hesitate to condescend and personally went to Chongqing to negotiate. Not only did Yu Liu refuse to return them, but also delayed and detained him for more than a month. After Provincial Liu returned to Chengdu, the kind of anger can be imagined. Yu Liu, feeling that the position of Southwest leader cannot be achieved through negotiation, also actively prepared for war, and also had a backstage and inside support (Tian Songyao), so his determination became more and more firm. In early October, he began his military operations.

Provincial Liu knew that the situation was not good, so he sang the theory of classmate cooperation, and at the same time showed leniency to Deng Tian, dividing three counties to Deng and three counties to Tian. However, Tian had an understanding with Liu Xiang long ago and stood on the same front (the Allied Army). On October 6, Tian's army first opened fire on Provincial Liu in Chengdu. Liu initially refused to fight back, but still did not reverse Tian's army commander's heart, taking advantage of the Allied Army's victories in the front line and Provincial Liu's concessions to think that by coercion, it would not be difficult for Provincial Liu to submit, and the whole army withdrew from the city, sitting back and profiting from the situation. So he repeatedly made provocations, but Provincial Liu firmly held the determination to survive with the city or perish with the city, and was not moved in the slightest. The Chengdu street fighting was inevitable and opened on November 15 at 1:30 p.m.

Chengdu's special situation is not only unique in the country, but also in the world.

The circumference of Chengdu City is about 28 li. Most of the city walls are still intact. Historically, it is divided into the Main City and the Minor City. The Main City is Chengdu, and the Minor City was originally the Manchu City. The Main City occupies about two-thirds of the east. The area inside the East Gate (East Street Chunxi Road) is the location of industry and commerce. The roads are wide, the electric lights shine at night, and the pedestrians are crowded. The Xisi Archway in Beiping is not as good as two or three of them. The Minor City is like the commercial port of Shenyang, where the residences of the general dignitaries are located, and there is no industry and commerce. This is nothing special.

Its special feature is in the administrative organization, which is slightly revealed. One city is the territory of two counties. The southeast part is the territory of Huayang, with the Huayang County Government. The northwest part is the territory of Chengdu County, with the Chengdu County Government. Above the two county governments, there is also a Municipal Government. Above the Municipal Government, there is also a Provincial Government. The Provincial Government also has three Military Governments (Three Army Headquarters). The Three Military Governments can be said to be the Supreme Government.

In terms of public security, its special feature is relatively clear. Each street has its own Regiment Affairs Office, funded by the residents of each street, raising a few old, weak, and opium-faced soldiers to maintain the public security of the street. Above this, there are also the police of the Municipal Government. Above the police, there are also the military police of the Provincial City Military Police Joint Office. Further up, there are soldiers directly dispatched by the military headquarters of various armies. These soldiers can also be said to be the Supreme Soldiers.

The most special thing is in the military defense zone. One city is divided into three defense zones. Generally speaking, before the war, the Twenty-fourth Army occupied the area inside the South Gate and the area inside the East Gate. The Twenty-eighth Army occupied the area inside the North Gate and the area inside the West Gate. The rest was the defense zone of the Twenty-ninth Army. Looking at it in more detail, there may still be the defense area of the Twenty-ninth Army within the defense area of the Twenty-fourth Army. It is intricate and difficult to investigate. The defense zones of various armies are absolutely like independent countries. The internal administrative personnel, such as the county government personnel, are appointed by the military headquarters and listen to the command of the military headquarters. The internal tax revenue is collected by the military headquarters. The internal public security is managed by the military headquarters. The police and the military police of the Military Police Joint Office are nothing more than deaf ears. The police can be said to be the most pitiful in the country. They don't even have socks on their feet. They wear light yellow military uniforms and hold a mourning stick. They don't even dare to stand on the street. They secretly hide in the shops. If a murder occurs, the murderer runs from this military district to that military district, and nothing happens. Even murders and robberies in broad daylight are not investigated. The people are really the straw dogs of the warlords, and their lives and property have no guarantee at all.

Under such a situation, Provincial Liu is naturally uneasy, and Deng Tian has also felt forced in recent years, and there is no way to live in peace for a long time, so war is inevitable.

×××

The Chengdu street fighting, from the afternoon of November 15 to the morning of November 24, was the most intense in the first two days, fighting for 24 hours at a stretch, without stopping for a moment. Cannons, machine guns, and grenades were used simultaneously, rumbling in the ears. Thinking of the lost land and the representatives of the League of Nations, I couldn't help but shed tears. The focus of the two armies' operations was initially in two places: (1) the headquarters of the Twenty-fourth Army; (2) the Imperial City; and later the arsenal outside the East Gate was added.

The headquarters of the Twenty-fourth Army, i.e., the former Governor-General's Office, is located at the junction of the Minor City and the Main City. Not far to its north is the defense zone of the Twenty-ninth Army. The mansion of its师长(Division Commander) Zeng Nanfu is on Kuixinglou Street, very close to the headquarters. The front, back, left, and right fire lines are the densest here. The streets and alleys are full of piles of stone slabs, like a wall.

The Imperial City, according to folklore, is the遗城(remnant city) of Liu Houzhu. It was still intact at the end of the Qing Dynasty. After more than a month of bombing in the second year of the Republic of China, only a South Gate, a North Gate, and a large mound of earth, known as Coal Mountain, remain. From the South Gate to the North Gate are all schools. On both sides of the South Gate are two middle schools, in the middle is the College of Liberal Arts and the College of Education of Sichuan University, and behind it are the affiliated primary school, Minxin Middle School, and the male department of the Art School.

The Imperial City has a very high terrain. Standing on Coal Mountain or the city gate, you can overlook the entire city, so it is a strategically important place. The arsenal, outside the East Gate, is the source of life for the Twenty-ninth Army. It is said that there are usually more than 2,000 people working inside, and guns and bullets can be manufactured.

The next important place is Shaanxi Street, not far from the Imperial City, where the Liu Mansion is located.

Except for the first two days, most of the rest were resting during the day and firing at night. The reporter lived in the Law School of the South Campus inside the South Gate and was always very safe.

×××

According to the announcement issued on the 24th, the Twenty-ninth Army accepted Deng Xihou's mediation, allowed the troops to withdraw from the city, and said that order had now been restored. However, it was difficult to pass through everywhere. It was not until yesterday (the 25th) afternoon that I was able to travel around everywhere. The headquarters of the Twenty-fourth Army did not suffer major losses. It is a pity that the surrounding civilian houses, Sichuan University in the Imperial City, and the two middle schools in front have not suffered any losses. The most severely damaged were the affiliated primary school, Minxin Middle School, and the Art School, most of which were burned. Those that were not burned were full of gun holes, broken walls, and it was so sad. Further back (out of the door), the Yuxi Bian Street was even more miserably fought. This street is where the small businesses and rickshaw pullers are located. It has already been unspeakable suffering on weekdays. Now the nests are pierced through the sky, and the objects have disappeared. How can they live? Some children are crying with hunger and cold, and their mothers are shedding clear tears and sighing up to the sky. Some are three-inch wooden coffins lying in front of the door, their wives are heartbroken and crying, not knowing what to say. Some are Taoists chanting sutras with a clanging sound, sending off this secluded soul. Some mothers have died and their fathers are still alive, leaving a group of orphans. Some are circling around the room, crying and weeping. Some are staring straight with both eyes, as if waking up from a Nanke dream, adding the opium addicts still lying in the open air and eating opium, adding the hairy toilets with fecal smells filling the nose. The eighteenth layer of hell is probably nothing more than this.

But there is something even more heartbreaking, and that is at the east end of Yuxi Bian Street, a woman crying with snot, tears, and saliva, crying to the death. Her husband died early. Her only hope was her six-year-old beloved son (who was shot to death. Her only pig, which she had worked so hard to raise, was also slaughtered and eaten by the army. Now the four walls are empty. This is at No. 196 Dongyu Hebei Street, (next to the Imperial City), in a very beautiful foreign-style house, a total of six coffins are parked. An old woman is crying with her head in her arms. From her crying, I heard that one [Blank] is a good husband, two are her sons, and two are her daughters: The world is sad for it, who will avenge the wronged souls:

But: Strange, there is really nothing strange about it. It is said that the two army commanders Tian and Liu are cooperating again. During the street fighting, the call for this cooperation was also discovered twice, and the two army commanders also crossed over:

It is also said that Tian Songyao is still connected with Yu Liu and is now temporarily withdrawing from the city, waiting for the Allied forces to approach Chengdu before making a comeback.

In the end, we don't know what stage it will reach. Even the authorities don't know. What we can know, and the authorities themselves also know, is "everything is shifted according to individual status."

The streets are plastered with slogans such as "Down with Tian Songyao" because he (1) violates public opinion, (2) destroys peace, (3) provokes the Sichuan war, (4) colludes with Liu Xiang, etc. Before the ink was dry, the notice protecting the residences of the officers of the Twenty-ninth Army was brilliantly revealed.

The generals of the Twenty-eighth Army and the generals of the Twenty-ninth Army telegraphed to advise the generals of the Twenty-fourth Army to abandon the dark and turn to the light, saying, "Don't be personal running dogs, be the army of the country." How firm it is, how passionate it is. But in the blink of an eye, the generals of the Twenty-eighth Army sang neutrality again. Army Commander Deng is once again running for peace with the aim of compassion: (November 26 in Chengdu)

Page 8

Shanghai and Guangdong Central Committee Members Travel to Beijing Together 83

He Yingqin and Others Left Last Night

Sun Ke and Others Have Not Decided on a Date

The Central News Agency reporter visited Central Committee Member Sun Zhesheng at his private residence yesterday to inquire about when he would go to Beijing to attend the Third Plenary Session of the Fourth Central Committee. According to him, the Third Plenary Session is of great importance to the country's future, so he has decided to go to Beijing to attend and jointly discuss national affairs. It has been decided that he will go to Beijing within the next two or three days. Most of the Central Committee members in Shanghai will go to Beijing to attend. Committee Member Song Qingling does not intend to attend. Regarding the issue of proposals, he has already drafted several proposals, but according to the order recently issued by the Central Committee, all proposals from Central Committee members must be registered by the Secretariat of the Third Plenary Session and officially announced, so he cannot disclose them now. However, the content is based on the national salvation program he had previously drafted. According to the reporter's investigation, Sun originally planned to take the night train to Beijing on the 14th to attend the opening ceremony of the Third Plenary Session on the morning of the 15th. However, due to matters that needed to be delayed, it has now been decided that he will accompany the Central Committee members in Shanghai Wu Chaochu, Zhang Huichang, Ma Chaojun, Chen Ce, Liang Hancao, Fu Rulin, and others on the night express train to Beijing on the 15th. As for Bai Wenwei, Li Liejun, Xiong Kewu, Zhang Zhiben, Yang Shukan, and others, the date of departure has not yet been decided. He Yingqin, Wu Tiecheng, Zeng Zhongming, Zhang Jingjiang, and others have already taken the night train to Beijing last night to attend.

The Guangdong Committee members Guan Su Ren, Deng Qingyang, Guang Xiu, and Li Qia'an have also taken the night train to Beijing last night. According to Guan Su Ren, before his departure, he told reporters that he had a meeting with Mr. Sun Zhesheng and other Shanghai Committee members last night (i.e., the night before last) to discuss the date of going to Beijing and attendance issues. Regarding the date of going to Beijing, it was decided that the committee members would go to Beijing in batches within one or two days. As for the proposals, Mr. Sun Zhesheng has drafted two proposals: one on concentrating national strength to save the crisis, and the other on the implementation of the party and government guidelines. The Shanghai and Guangdong Committee members will jointly sign them and submit them to the plenary session for discussion.

Xu Du-bi's Statement 84

Will Definitely Not Attend the Third Plenary Session

Feng Yuxiang Sells His House

A reporter from the Guowen News Agency visited Central Committee member Xu Du-bi yesterday and asked him when he would go to Beijing to attend the meeting and about Feng Yuxiang's repeated telegrams of correction. Xu stated the following: I do not intend to go to Beijing to attend the meeting. Since the September 18th National Crisis, anyone with even a little patriotic spirit has been willing to abandon internal and personal prejudices, unite sincerely, and save us from peril. Therefore, at the First Plenary Session in Nanjing in January of this year and the Second Plenary Session in Luoyang in March, I attended with a full heart and a spirit of knowing no bounds in speaking my mind. However, the result was not only useless but also caused many misunderstandings, which I find very painful to think about. This time, when the Third Plenary Session convenes, I should attend, but if I attend without speaking, I would be as silent as a cicada, which would be meaningless. If I speak my mind fully, it will inevitably cause more misunderstandings, not to mention that even if I speak, it may not be effective. Therefore, after careful consideration, I think it would be better not to attend. After Mr. Feng arrived in Zhangjiakou, although

little news has been heard, colleagues and friends who have received letters have said that whenever Mr. Feng moves to a new place, the outside world speculates in various ways, creating illusions out of thin air. For example, when he first moved from Xuzhou to Mount Tai, there were all sorts of rumors. After he lived there for a long time, the rumors subsided. Later, when the war in eastern Shandong broke out, Mr. Feng moved to Zhangjiakou to avoid rumors, but unexpectedly, rumors arose again because of this. Is this oversensitive speculation, or is it malicious slander from someone with ulterior motives, which is exhausting. Mr. Feng is free to live wherever he wants, and if people in society recognize this, rumors will naturally not arise. Furthermore, if Mr. Feng has rumors when he lives in Zhangjiakou, who can guarantee that there will be no rumors if he moves to other places?

Currently, Mr. Feng is in financial difficulty and is planning to sell two houses he bought in previous years, namely the library where he currently lives and Ai Wu Lu. After this matter is settled, he may move elsewhere, which is also possible.

Wage Increase Crisis Among Employees on Two Railways 85

Preventing Hangzhou Train from Leaving for Shanghai

Resolved Only After Great Effort

Employees at all stations along the entire Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway line, due to the issue of wage increases for January and February of this year, repeatedly requested equal treatment for all employees and sent more than 50 representatives from various stations to the head office to petition. They did not receive a concrete and satisfactory result. Yesterday morning around 8 o'clock, workers from the gate station, vehicle section, and engine section in Hangzhou, feeling that the end of the year was approaching and there was still no hope of a concrete solution, gathered dozens of employees from stations such as the gate, Nanxing, and Hangzhou to come to Shanghai to continue their petition, requesting that the vehicle section allocate a special train. The vehicle section did not dare to assign one without authorization, which caused a disturbance. At that time, the thirty-ninth fourth-class passenger train from the gate to Hangzhou was being fitted with the engine to depart, leading a crowd of workers to sit on the tracks at the station to prevent the engine from moving. Later, leaders from the engine and vehicle sections did their best to persuade and comfort them, asking them not to take actions outside the rails, to work peacefully, and to wait quietly for a batch order, as there would be a solution for equal treatment for all. The employees then withdrew from the tracks, and the thirty-ninth slow train for third and fourth-class passengers was able to depart for Shanghai. In addition to being delayed at the station for an hour, the third and fourth-class passenger train arrived at the Shanghai station about two hours late.

Public Prosecution Filed Against Chen Fumu and Li Guojie, Former General Manager and Supervisor of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company 86

▲ Criminal Suspicions Are All Clear

▲ Malfeasance and Breach of Trust Combined for Conviction

Li Guojie, former general manager of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and Chen Fumu, former Deputy Minister of Communications and concurrent supervisor, were reported by Minister of Communications Zhu Jia-hua for using the three wharves of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to borrow foreign debt from the American company China Sales Company without authorization. Li Guojie was detained and sent to a Shanghai hospital for treatment due to illness. The local court actively investigated the case, collecting evidence such as bank deposits, and concluded that the criminal suspicions of the defendants Li Guojie and Chen Fumu were all clear. A public prosecution has now been filed. The criminal articles cited in the indictment are Article 140 of the Criminal Code (aggravated offense by taking advantage of one's position) and Article 366 of the same law (breach of trust), and they will be combined for conviction according to Article 70.

▲ Implementation Can Be Approved Once the Attached Schedule Is Agreed Upon

The Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce reported that the silk and satin industry and the electrical silk weaving industry associations stated in their letters that the Vietnamese government was imposing excessive taxes on silk fabrics, making it impossible for Chinese silk to be sold in Vietnam. It is now known that the Chamber received a reply from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs yesterday: The presentation is noted. The Sino-French Vietnamese Special Convention has not been approved and implemented for a long time because the attached schedule has not yet been agreed upon. The Ministry is now actively negotiating this attached schedule with the French side. Once it is finalized, the convention can be approved and implemented by both parties. Please be informed of this. This is the reply.

Dai Jien, New Manager of China National Aviation Corporation, Took Office Yesterday 88

Dai went to the company yesterday morning at 10 o'clock to take office. No ceremony was held at the time. Dai only summoned his subordinates to talk, inquiring about important matters in the company. Chen Xinghan, Director of Two Railways Bureaus, Suddenly Resigned Yesterday 89

Chen Xinghan, Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway Bureaus, suddenly submitted his resignation to the Ministry of Railways yesterday, stating that he had been in a busy and stressful position for a long time, his mind and body were exhausted, and he earnestly requested to resign from the positions of Director of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Bureaus, hoping that the Ministry would approve his request so that he could recuperate. He humbly stated that he had been appointed by the Ministry to take over as Director of the Two Railway Bureaus because the Shanghai Incident had just erupted, the country was facing a national crisis, and the Two Railways were in a crucial position, related to the overall strategy of foreign resistance and military affairs, and could not be without a responsible person for a single day. He was motivated by a sense of duty and reluctantly came forward to maintain the situation. Therefore, during the military period, although he experienced many dangers and dealt with difficult situations, he still worked hard to maintain military transportation, so that the front-line combat would not be disrupted due to transportation interruptions, and to rescue railway property, so that more than one hundred locomotives and vehicles left behind in the North Station area would not be used by the enemy. In addition, he rescued refugees, maintained transportation, and protected merchants' goods, doing everything within his power. After the war ceased and negotiations began, he realized that restoring transportation on the Beijing-Shanghai Railway was of utmost importance to the country's politics, social economy, and international perception, so he started working on repairs to railway stations and planning train schedules. He worked tirelessly and slept little, and finally restored full line traffic on the day the enemy troops withdrew. At that time, after accumulating fatigue, he originally intended to retire after the task was completed to recuperate. Thinking that although traffic had been restored, construction still needed to be planned and maintained, and that the Shanghai Main Station was the hub of the Two Railways, it was necessary to quickly restore it. Therefore, he forgot his limitations and, based on his daily experience and observations, prepared a report on the restoration of the Shanghai Main Station and submitted it to the Ministry, hoping to contribute to the effort. Fortunately, the Ministry adopted it and convened a Two Railways Construction and Restoration Committee. At the meeting, the general plan was decided and only awaited implementation. Since Chen Xinghan took over the position until now, for several months, he had been loyal in times of crisis and followed regulations in routine matters, never daring to neglect his duties, which had caused him great effort and concern. Now that railway affairs had returned to normal and construction was expected to be completed soon, he humbly submitted this document to explain the situation and earnestly requested that he be allowed to resign and that a capable person be selected to take over as soon as possible to emphasize railway affairs, so that he could rest and recuperate and plan to repay the country in the future. He was overwhelmed with gratitude and awaited orders.

After discussing everything, he arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and stayed at the French Consulate General. Director Huang of the 19th Route Army in Beijing Arrives in Shanghai 91

To Inspect Wounded Soldiers

There are still more than 40 wounded soldiers of the 19th Route Army, who bravely resisted the Japanese, recuperating in Shanghai, residing in the Pingmin Convalescent Hospital at the intersection of Weihaiwei Road and Chongqing Road. It is learned that Huang Hechun, director of the army's office in Beijing, is very concerned about these soldiers wounded for the country and came to Shanghai in person the day before yesterday to express his sympathy and inspect their injuries. Medical Director Mou Hongyi and Administrative Director Liu Daofang accompanied him to each ward to inspect them one by one. Director Huang expressed his warm condolences to the wounded soldiers, advising them to rest in peace. In several cases where residual shrapnel remained in their bodies and had not been completely removed, Huang approved a second operation to allow them to recover as soon as possible.

French Scholar Pellet Arrives in Shanghai 92

▲ Plans to Stay in Shanghai for Two Weeks Before Going to Beijing

According to the North-China Daily News, French scholar Pellet, a professor at the Collège de France, has been studying Chinese affairs for decades and is known as a China expert. He arrived in Shanghai aboard the French mail steamer Zhen Nusha. This trip followed a visit to Vietnam, where he stayed briefly, postponing his ship by one voyage. It is reported that Pellet is on a mission from the French Ministry of Public Education and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. According to his interview with reporters, although his last visit to Vietnam was thirteen years ago, he has maintained close contact with the country since he established the École Française d'Extrême-Orient in Vietnam thirty-three years ago and is familiar with the situation there. Listening to him talk about Vietnam today, even decades ago, feels like yesterday. After landing at Penang on the postal steamer Alami, he traveled through Bangkok, Angor, and then to Jinta City, Sisek, and Hue-Hanoi. Although he traveled in haste, he was able to gain insight into the development of the area by visiting the museum and the archaeological research institute. He has now reached the main goal of his trip by arriving in China. China is a country he deeply loves and has devoted his life to studying its culture. He aims to increase opportunities for contact between scholars of the two countries and to observe China's achievements from a scholarly perspective, thereby enhancing academic cooperation between the two countries. He currently plans to stay in Shanghai for two weeks before going to Beijing for a short stay of two months.

Secretary-General Yu Talks About the Recent Situation of the Municipal Administration 93

Secretary-General Yu of the Municipal Government spoke to reporters yesterday about various recent situations in the municipal administration, as follows:

Municipal Financial Tightening Issue

Due to the impact of the war, the Shanghai Municipal Government's budget for this year has a deficit of more than one million yuan in income and expenditure. In addition, due to the expenses of the security team, the budget has increased by one million yuan, making the treasury even more stretched. Therefore, in order to tighten finances, Director Cai raised the issue at the 222nd municipal meeting. It was decided that I, Director Cai, and Commissioner Xu would work together to find remedial measures. The measures that have now been agreed upon are as follows: 1. Increase revenue. There has always been a division of troops stationed in this city for security, and its expenses have been borne by the central government. This year, due to the need to suppress the communists, the troops were transferred elsewhere, and the local police force felt thin, so the security team was organized. The annual expenses are about one million yuan. At a time when income is short, the municipal government really cannot afford this huge sum. Therefore, it is planned to request the central government to allocate funds separately for the security team's expenses, which will surely be approved by the central government. 2. Reduce expenditure. To make up for the deficit of more than one million yuan, expenditure will be reduced. All bureaus and affiliated institutions should strive to save as much as possible in all areas where savings are possible. All temporary expenses that have been approved by the municipal government but have not been paid should be listed by the Finance Bureau and submitted to the mayor for review, distinguishing between priorities and moderately reducing or delaying them. If the above two measures can be implemented, the municipal treasury deficit may be temporarily made up.

Municipal Bank Expansion Issue 94

Since its establishment, the Municipal Bank has not been able to develop fully due to a lack of capital. However, its credit has been established, and there is a slight surplus every year. If it can be actively expanded, its future prospects are unlimited. Mayor Wu, in view of this, has decided to expand the original capital of one million yuan to six million yuan, separately soliciting three million yuan in commercial shares and three million yuan from the municipal government. In addition to the original capital of one million yuan, one million yuan will be disbursed from the Fuxing Public Bonds, and the remaining one million yuan will be transferred from the municipal government's profit-making enterprises.

Municipal Ferry Expansion Issue 95

As for the expansion plan of the municipal ferry, which requires 300,000 yuan, a corresponding method has also been discussed and handed over to the Finance and Land Bureaus for consultation and implementation. Since the municipal ferry was established, its business has been developing and its income has been increasing. In addition to expenses and replenishment, there is a considerable surplus. If the expansion plan is successful, it will not only benefit the transportation of citizens but also generate profits in the future.

Petition Representatives from the Anti-Civil War Association Will Go to Beijing Tonight 96

The Association Issued a Public Telegram Yesterday

Stating Liu Xiang's Crimes

The General Assembly of the Anti-Civil War League, after deciding at the third meeting of the Standing Committee the day before yesterday to announce non-cooperation with Liu Xiang for violating the orders of the National Government and continuing the civil war, convened a meeting of the daily Standing Committee members at 1:30 pm yesterday to discuss the telegram that should be sent. Wang Xiaolai, Lin Kanghou, Du Yuesheng, Liu Zhanen (representing Xu Jiqing), Wu Daquan (representing Qian Xinzhi), Yan Esheng, and others attended. After discussing various telegrams, they were sent separately. Furthermore, the representatives to Beijing, Lin Kanghou and Liu Zhanen, are scheduled to take the night train to Beijing at 11:30 tonight, carrying a petition to petition the Third Plenary Session.

The association issued a public telegram yesterday (with title omitted):

For your review. The national crisis is becoming increasingly urgent, and we have no time to resist foreign aggression. If anyone has a heart, how can they bear internal strife? Since its establishment, this association has been working hard to achieve the goal of domestic stability and foreign resistance with the united strength of the people. Unexpectedly, in mid-September of this year, this association repeatedly received reports from Sichuanese in Shanghai stating that both Chengdu and Chongqing were making military movements, fearing that misfortune would occur, and requesting that methods be devised to eliminate it. This association believes that at this time of national salvation, we should not have internal conflicts. If the authorities in Sichuan can make a clear statement, then it can prove that the accusers are wrong. Therefore, on September, telegrams were sent to Chengdu Military Commander Liu Wenhui and Chongqing Military Commander Liu Xiang, asking them to respond quickly by telegram to reassure the people. Soon, Military Commander Liu Wenhui replied by telegram, stating that Wenhui was internally seeking harmony, compromising himself for the sake of others, and that this was his consistent goal, witnessed by the gods. Even if people do not understand me, I will try to avoid it. However, I can make concessions and never start a war, etc. Military Commander Liu Xiang also replied by telegram, stating how could we kill each other and lightly start a war? The military action you inquired about is completely fictitious. It is just that there are many rumors and some people may be dissatisfied and intend to provoke, etc. This association carefully examined the wording of the two telegrams. Although the meanings were different, they were consistent in denying the war. We immediately announced it. By early October, the rumors became even more urgent. This association sent telegrams to both parties again, asking them to quickly order their troops not to act rashly. After the telegram was sent, Liu Wenhui responded to the telegram again, stating that he could settle disputes internally and would not hesitate to make compromises. He still hoped that those who are greedy and rebellious would awaken so as not to betray his sincere teachings, etc. However, Liu Xiang did not respond. Not long after, the war broke out. This association sent letters and telegrams, urging a cessation of hostilities, but to no avail. Even when the central conference and the ministry telegraphed to stop the war, and the National Government issued a clear order to cease fire on November, it not only failed to move the listeners who were inciting chaos, but it even intensified. Even street fighting occurred in the provincial capital, and the city was turned into rubble, with more than 40,000 houses destroyed and more than 10,000 citizens killed, opening up an unprecedented catastrophe in Sichuan in three hundred years. This association repeatedly received reports and was extremely pained and angry. At the same time, the International League of Nations was holding a conference in Geneva, and our country's representatives were striving to uphold justice. But looking back at the domestic situation, it was as if our enemies were pleased and our friends were regretful. Who is responsible for this? The crime cannot be concealed. On the 23rd of last month, this association again received a telegram from Military Commander Liu Wenhui stating the course of his retreat, voluntarily giving up defenses everywhere, hoping that someone would uphold justice and resolve the dispute as soon as possible. This association immediately sent the telegram to the National Government Military Council Military and Political Department, reiterating strict orders to generals on all sides to instruct their troops to abide by the government's order to cease fire and asking Military Commander Liu Xiang to express his agreement with the peace proposal and jointly plan for a settlement. After the telegram was sent, we received a reply from the Military Council, stating that the Sichuan war was being resolved, but there was still no indication from Military Commander Liu Xiang. According to reports in the newspapers in recent days, Military Commander Liu Xiang has scheduled a general offensive, and the war has intensified again. The failure to stop the Sichuan war this time is attributable to him, and there is no denying it. Furthermore, according to the Shanghai newspapers, a telegram from Chengdu on November 12 stated that Rongzhang Municipal Elementary School teachers and students were propagating the abolition of war and were arrested by Wang Zanxu's troops of the Chongqing Army, detained in the headquarters, and the leading student, Shen Xuanheng, was immediately executed. Not only that, but the Chongqing telegram on December 2 stated that after the Xinshu Daily published the National Government's order to cease fire, it was investigated and sealed by the garrison department, and people in Sichuan mediated, and the person in charge wrote a letter of repentance to settle the matter. It is that Military Commander Liu Xiang not only stopped the people's anti-civil war movement, but also resented the National Government's ceasefire order and vented his anger on the Xinshu Daily. What about the protection of human rights? What about freedom of speech? On the same day, a telegram from Chongqing stated that Liu Xiang had detained Lan Wenbin, a brigade commander of the 21st Army, for opposing the civil war for 20 days and executed him by shooting on December 1. Furthermore, the Yutong Bank, which has strong capital, was sealed by Liu Xiang because it did not underwrite the third phase of financial public bonds, all cash was confiscated, and the manager was imprisoned. If he disregarded everything, was fond of chaos by nature, and acted arbitrarily and violently, he was directly intolerable to the national law and public opinion. According to Article 2, Item 3 of the association's constitution, if a civil war unfortunately occurs, the association's group members and individual members should unanimously refuse to cooperate. It was specially approved by the third meeting of the Standing Committee on the 10th of this month that the crimes of Liu Xiang, who violated the orders of the National Government, continued the civil war, sealed newspapers and banks, and shot students, should be announced in a telegram, and it was formally decided not to cooperate with Liu Xiang. For this purpose, this special telegram is sent to you. We request that the central government use its administrative power to severely sanction and dismiss him from all positions, which should not be tolerated. We also hope that the people's groups and public opinion organs across the country will express their views and jointly condemn him. Members of this association should especially earnestly implement the association's charter and refuse any cooperation with Liu Xiang to ensure that this criminal of civil war, who divides the country and causes chaos, is intolerable to the people of the whole country, and is subject to severe condemnation, more severe than axes and halberds. We offer these painful words in the hope that you will take note. The third standing committee of the General Alliance for the Abolition of Civil War: Standing members Wang Xiaolai, Du Yuesheng, Lin Kanghou, Wu Daquan, Liu Zhanen, Qian Xinzhi, Lu Jianquan, Pu Xinya, Jin Jianquan, Song Yuting, Chen Liting, Zhou Zuomin, Chen Peide, Leng Zhanqi, Yang Meizhen, Li Gongpu, Hu Shuhua, Fu Yueqi, Li Denghui, Yuan Songxun, Liu Shimu, Wang Yansong, Yu Xiaochuan, Xu Huaiqing, Wang Yi, Li Kuian, Yan Esheng, Yu Rongqiao, Lin Junbao, Chen Shi, Ma Wenhui, Xu Jiqing, Chen Zheqing, Lu Zhangyuan, Di , Zhou Xuexiang, Zhu Xuefan kowtow,

They are constantly fighting the enemy in the freezing cold, enduring hardships and sacrificing their lives on the battlefield. We are deeply grateful for your enthusiastic assistance. We have repeatedly received letters and telegrams from the front describing their suffering and urgently requesting us to appeal to all sectors for assistance and relief. The language is urgent and filled with tears, making it unbearable to read. We have disclosed it to various newspapers from time to time, inviting your attention. We still earnestly request the association to consider and allocate funds for relief, so that the spirit of loyalty and righteousness may be upheld and the success of the restoration may be achieved. This is our earnest hope."

▲ Yuan Chonggu's Visit: Yuan Chonggu, Commander of the Reclamation Army and Brigade Commander of the First Artillery Brigade of Heilongjiang, and Front-Line Commander of the Jiangqiao, along with Wai Guang and Li Shiyong, visited the Volunteer Army Support Association yesterday. It was also heard that Yuan is currently under the command of Pu Bingshan.

▲ Visiting Hours: To facilitate meetings with Northeastern Volunteer Army leaders and representatives who have come to Shanghai for negotiations, the association has designated Mondays, Tuesdays, and Fridays from 4:00 PM to 6:00 PM as visiting hours. The executive directors will take turns to receive visitors. The schedule is as follows: Wu Shan, Fu, Yu Cheng on Mondays; Li Cishan, Feng Shaoshan, Li Shaochuan, and Du Yongyuan on Wednesdays; and Jiang Wenyu, Chu Hui Seng, Yan Zhifang, and Chen Yafu on Fridays. Reorganization and Establishment of the Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe Volunteer Army Transportation Corps Yesterday 101

He Yuanhun's Unit Guiding the Reorganization

Office Located in the Chenxiangge Today

The Northeastern Volunteer Army Transportation Corps, after being ordered to cease activities by the Municipal Public Security Bureau, initially planned to disband immediately, temporarily dismissing all staff and awaiting an opportunity. However, all the initiators of the corps, over a dozen people, intended to go out to the passes to join the Volunteer Army out of their patriotic aspirations. He Yuanhun, Commander-in-Chief of the Rehe National Salvation Army, commissioned Bo Wei, Commander of the Sixth Route Army, and Liu Daxiong, Counselor of the Sixty-First Division of the Nineteenth Route Army, believing that the corps's organizational purpose was perfectly suited to the needs of the Volunteer Army, felt it was a pity to stop it. Therefore, they explained the misunderstanding to the authorities, who approved its establishment and guided the resumption of work, renaming it the Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe Volunteer Army Transportation Corps. The initiators of the corps, Zheng Jianbo and others, expressed their gratitude and immediately found an office location at the Chenxiangge on Dajichang Street, and it was decided to start working today.

▲ Talking about the Relief Situation Outside the Passes

After the first batch of members of the Northeastern Volunteer Army Medical Team arrived in Jinxi, they immediately started medical work in the Qi Jizhou unit of the Volunteer Army on the Fourth Road in Jinxi.
