According to You Chunsheng, after the news of the Soviet army's withdrawal spread, the Volunteer Armies on all fronts were extremely indignant and willing to fight to the last ditch against the Japanese invaders. They are currently training soldiers and horses, and will issue an attack order within days. Therefore, there is an urgent need for medical supplies. He was specially sent to Shanghai to contact the rear, and he will return to the front as soon as the medicines are ready. He also said that it has been snowing in the area since November 4, and the Volunteer Army medical team is still working in the freezing cold wearing only thin cotton clothes. Therefore, he hopes that all sectors will find ways to provide assistance, so that the comrades at the front can serve with peace of mind.

The Shareholders' Rights Protection Association of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Hosted the Press Yesterday 103

Opposing the Government's Acquisition of Shares at Fifty Taels

Will Send Representatives to Petition the Third Plenary Session in Beijing

According to the Guowen News Agency, since the government issued an order to prepare funds to take back the state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, the shareholders of the company have risen up to form a Legal Rights Protection Association to study the interests of the shareholders. Yesterday, the association held a tea party for the press at the Ningbo Tongxiang Association in Shanghai on Xizang Road, attended by dozens of people. During the meeting, Li Zhengwu, the organizer of the association, first stood up to report the purpose of inviting the reporters and said that he hoped that the media would uphold public opinion. Then, Li Cishan stood up to report the origin of the Shareholders' Rights Protection Association and to request the government to take into account the interests of the shareholders. The speech is as follows:

Chairman Li Cishan reported on behalf of the association: "We are all shareholders holding shares in the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Accumulated Assets Company. Our shares are traded annually without a market, but the assets of our two major companies are valuable. According to reports from experts and responsible personnel, there are indeed huge sums of 50 million to 70 million taels. Recently, we saw the order from the National Government, according to the proposal of the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Transportation, to decide to return the shares of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to state ownership, giving each set of shares a price of fifty taels. We, the people, do not have much to say about this strict order from the government. However, we heard an ancient saying, 'In a country ruled by law, orders cannot change laws.' We, the shareholders of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, remember that on December 21, 1929, the National Government issued a glorious order, 'The Regulations on the Supervision of Public Utility Enterprises Operated by Private Individuals are hereby formulated and promulgated.' Article 2, paragraph 5 of these regulations specifically includes the two words 'shipping.' Our China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, operated by private individuals, is naturally a public utility enterprise operated by private individuals subject to these regulations. These regulations are our golden rules, so we cannot but remember them firmly. Articles 14 and 15 of these regulations stipulate the methods for returning enterprises to public ownership. Article 14 was amended once on February 7, 1931. The current text is: 'Article 14. After thirty years from the establishment of a public utility enterprise operated by private individuals, the supervisory authority may take it back into public ownership at a price, but must notify one year in advance.' Article 14, paragraph 2, states: 'For public utility enterprises operated by private individuals established before the implementation of these regulations, after thirty years from the implementation of these regulations, the provisions of the preceding paragraph may be used to take them back into public ownership. If the time limit is shorter, it shall be in accordance with its regulations.' Article 15 states: 'When a public utility enterprise operated by private individuals is taken back into public ownership, it shall be paid according to the price assessed by experts based on the total amount of its existing assets.' Article 15, paragraph 2, states: 'If there is a disagreement with the aforementioned valuation, the local court shall send one person, and the local autonomous group and the Chamber of Commerce shall each send two people to form a valuation committee to review and determine the price.' This is the law formally promulgated by our National Government. This law was promulgated and implemented on December 11, 1929. By November of this year, it will be two years and eleven months. According to the mandate given by the law, our China Merchants Steam Navigation Company operated by private individuals still has seventeen years and one month. Can it be taken back into public ownership immediately without notice, shortening its legal life? This is the first point we should study. The total amount of existing assets of our China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and the Accumulated Assets Company, according to expert reports, is more than 50 million taels. After deducting the repayment of debts, the assets owned by our shareholders, calculated at 84,000 shares, should be worth more than 600 taels per share. According to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Transportation's claim, calculated at 1,200 taels per set. Now, regardless of the total amount of our assets, let's just talk about the number of shares. The words 'total amount of existing assets' are still prominently displayed in the current law. I don't know what kind of law this method of calculating by set is based on. This is the second point we should study. The law clearly states that when taking it back into public ownership, it should be based on the total amount of its existing assets, according to the price assessed by experts. Now, we are given 50 taels of cash per set, and I don't know which expert's report this is based on, and whether it is the total amount calculated based on the value of those assets. This is the third point we should study. We hold shares in the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, and of course we hope that these shares will be protected by the law already granted to us. We are citizens of the Republic of China, and we especially hope that the laws of the Republic of China will maintain their due credibility and effectiveness. If the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Transportation want to propose amendments in advance, to return the company to public ownership, they are free to amend the law to whatever extent, or indefinitely, or without giving a price, as long as they follow the legislative procedure and promulgate and implement it, it will take effect. However, they did not do any work to amend the law. Under the very clear and detailed regulations mentioned earlier, they are depriving us of more than twenty-three years of legal rights without any basis. In order to protect our own interests, we cannot willingly endure this. In order to respect the use of national laws and the effectiveness of laws, we also need to discuss with the government and ask them to consider it. The reason why we organized the 'Shareholders' Rights Protection Association' is precisely for this."

Petitioning in Beijing

According to Li Cishan, although the association has not yet officially published a notice to register shareholdings, it has already received official letters and telegrams from shareholders stating that more than shares have been registered. The association plans to petition the government after reaching 20,000 registered households and will send representatives to Beijing to petition during the Third Plenary Session, and consult with the Supervisory Yuan and the Legislative Yuan on the issue of the government's takeover of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company.

The Special Branch of the Chinese Seamen's Party, due to the Japanese police's unauthorized arrest of Chinese seamen on the British ship "Russian Queen," sent a telegram to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Chinese Consulate in Nagasaki requesting negotiations with the Japanese side. We ordered personnel to investigate with the shipping company. Later, we received a report stating that a Japanese worker was injured due to an accident on the 'Russian Queen,' resulting in the detention of three Chinese seamen by the Japanese police, who have not yet been released. The incident has occurred more than a week ago. We dare not speculate on the current situation. If it is indeed true, we earnestly request your department to negotiate with the ambassador to Japan for their release and ensure that similar incidents do not occur in the future, so as to protect the safety of seamen. Notes on the Completion of the Dike Project by the National Flood Relief Association (13) 105

Chiang Individually Receives Visitors

At 10:30 AM on the 5th, Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, received Xu Shiying, Wen Lantao, Li Zushen, Qian Hua (representing this newspaper), Lu Yi (representing the Xinwen News), and Wan Shen Sun Faxu and Xu Guozhi, representatives of the Shanghai fundraising committee for the temporary disaster relief in Henan, Hubei, and Anhui provinces, at the Bandit Suppression Headquarters. At the same time, he also received four representatives of the Nanjing-Beiping disaster area inspection group in individual meetings. Due to his busy schedule, the conversation time was limited to three minutes. Xu and this newspaper's reporter arrived at the headquarters at 10:30 AM. After waiting in the reception room for a while, Chiang met them one by one. The details of the conversations are recorded separately below. 1. When Xu Shiying paid his respects, he first recounted the inspection of the dike project and the organization process of the disaster relief association in Jiangxin. Then, he reported four points: (1) Please ask the headquarters to send personnel to demarcate the inspection route of the bandit area. (2) All sectors in Shanghai have begun raising funds for the emergency disaster relief in the three provinces and will do their best to allocate funds for disaster relief in one county as soon as possible and actively carry out the relief in the fastest way. (3) The method is based entirely on the rural relief regulations issued by the Bandit Suppression Headquarters. (4) A portion of the surcharge on electricity and water can be allocated to disaster relief funds. Please ask the government to negotiate with Chairman Song. Chiang responded that Xu was already old and it was not appropriate for him to travel to the bandit area and endure all kinds of hardships. He asked him to return to Shanghai as soon as possible to take charge of everything. 2. When Wen Lantao met with Chiang, he said briefly that he was very satisfied with the dike project he had inspected along the way. It was rare to see such a historical project completed during the Commander-in-Chief's time. He hoped that the Commander-in-Chief would pay special attention to future protection. He also said that the Commander-in-Chief's bandit suppression was out of love for the people, and Lantao was now willing to ask for love for things, that is, the fish in the West Lake had been approved by the chairman of the Zhejiang Provincial Government to be released, but Mayor Zhao had disobeyed the order. Please ask the Commander-in-Chief to find a way to deal with it. Chiang immediately agreed and asked Wen not to travel far again. Wen said that the Commander-in-Chief was so hardworking and able to endure hardship. As a member of the people, how dare Lantao be afraid of hard work? 3. When Li Zushen paid his respects, he stated the necessity of external propaganda, such as the completion of this dike project, to show the world the efforts of the Chinese people and the cooperation between the government and the people, so that the post-disaster recovery could be done quickly.

Chiang's Talk

When Chiang met with this newspaper's reporter, he said that he would return to Beijing within a week to attend the Third Plenary Session and would come to Wuhan in about a month to preside over the bandit suppression. This newspaper's reporter asked the Commander-in-Chief whether he had any special proposals for the Third Plenary Session. (Answer) I am currently organizing them. (Question) Will they be submitted jointly with Mr. Wang? (Answer) Not yet decided. (Question) In terms of diplomacy, if the League of Nations cannot resolve the Sino-Japanese dispute, will the government determine its own response policy? (Answer) Regarding diplomatic matters, the government has determined a detailed response policy. (Question) In terms of domestic affairs, unity and sincerity are the main goals in times of national crisis. In your opinion, can it be done based on the current situation? (Answer) Given time, it can definitely be done. (Question) Can Mr. Hu Zhantang and the two gentlemen, Yan and Feng, go to Beijing to attend the First Plenary Session? (Answer) There has been no news recently. (Question) There are rumors that the Commander-in-Chief has formed a fascist and blue-shirt group. The headquarters has repeatedly corrected this, but the rumors have not stopped. What is the truth? (Answer) I have heard nothing about this. It is all unfounded rumors. Please tell the Shanghai press." The conversation time was long, and the reporter took his leave. (Qian Hua from Hankou, December 5)

Xing Zhigang Submits a Request to Yan Shenyu to Request the Provincial Office to Return Two Years of Borrowed Grain 107

Xing Zhigang, the Fifth District Chief of Shanghai County, yesterday submitted a report to the County Government, requesting that it be forwarded to the Provincial Office to allocate the prepaid Winter Dredging for the fifteenth and twentieth years to alleviate the people's difficulties. The report continued, requesting that the Provincial Office follow the original plan to allocate the prepaid winter grain to uphold national credibility and comfort the people's hopes. It was found that over the years, Jiangsu Province had borrowed winter grain in advance, accumulating a debt of four yuan and five jiao per stone. In the eighteenth year of the Republic of China, the Finance Department formulated a plan to allocate and repay it in installments over five years, from the nineteenth year to the twenty-third year, to be fully repaid as scheduled. The Provincial Government Committee decided to issue a public announcement in conjunction with the Finance Department, which can be verified. However, in the nineteenth year, due to insufficient provincial government budget, an order was received to postpone the repayment. In the twentieth year, the district was hit by continuous rain and disaster. After the autumn harvest, the district chief requested to allocate the pre-borrowed winter grain for the tenth and twentieth years to alleviate the disaster situation. The government issued the Finance Department Directive No. 4770, which stated: "The report is noted. Regarding the borrowed grain, according to the original plan, this department will repay it in full this year. However, this year's continuous rain and disaster have resulted in a significant shortfall in provincial revenue. If we return the borrowed grain, it will be even more difficult to sustain. This department has already submitted a report to the Provincial Government, which has decided to postpone it for one year. The order is to comply. Therefore, there is no need to protect it. You should immediately inform the district." Given the previous situation, a directive was issued to inform the district. It was noted that after this year's military disaster and famine, the people's morale was revived. Although the autumn harvest was relatively abundant, the price was surprisingly low, and the cotton consumption was reduced. It was insufficient to recover the losses of last year. The people's livelihood was deteriorating. The provincial government had already issued a clear order to postpone the repayment of borrowed grain for one year. In the minds of the people, national credibility could be maintained. When the one-year period expires, it should be repaid according to the plan. The eager expectation is like birds waiting to be fed. However, recently, the news of continued postponement of the winter grain levy has caused the people to lose hope and panic. The district chief witnessed the people's difficulties and, based on the township chiefs' inquiries, dared to request the governor to forward a report to the Provincial Office, approving the allocation of 1.8 yuan per stone of pre-borrowed winter grain for the nineteenth and twentieth years, in order to maintain national credibility and relieve the people's difficulties. This is truly a public service.

Joint Management of Radio Broadcasting in Concessions 108

The Shanghai Evening Post reported that the Shanghai radio broadcasting issue is expected to be resolved soon. It is rumored that this week, representatives from the Shanghai Municipal Council of the International Settlement and the French Municipal Council will meet with the Chinese Radio Administration to jointly manage all radio stations in China, including those in the Shanghai concessions. In the future, Nanjing will designate the call signs and wavelengths to be used. According to the current plan, radio stations in the International Settlement and the French Concession must first apply to the Chinese Radio Administration for the call signs and wavelengths to be used. Then, the radio stations in the concessions must register with the competent authorities. The Chinese Radio Administration is currently equipping itself with wave detection machinery. It is expected that the Chinese and foreign authorities will agree on a cooperative basis for joint management of radio stations in the concessions. If radio stations still arbitrarily disregard the designated wavelengths and disrupt radio waves, Chinese experts will investigate and provide evidence, and the foreign officials in charge of the concessions will stop them.

Mr. Massey of the Municipal Council Succeeds as a Member of the Health Committee 109

Mr. Leslie of the Municipal Council Health Committee previously requested leave to return to his home country. During his leave, the vacant position of the committee member was temporarily filled by Mr. P. W. Massey. Now that Mr. Leslie has returned to Shanghai, he has requested to resign from the committee. With Mr. Massey's consent, the Board of Directors agreed to allow him to continue to serve. Therefore, the Board of Directors unanimously decided to appoint Mr. Massey to fill the vacancy until the end of the current municipal year.

Fire on Milu Road, One Person Burned to Death 112

The body has become charred

The tragic scene is heartbreaking

No. 4, Ronghua Lane, Milu Road, French Concession, is a building with three floors above ground and two side rooms. In the east side room downstairs, a man surnamed Xu runs a toy shop, using sulfur ammunition to make toy guns for children. He hires male and female workers to teach people how to make small dots of ammunition on paper. Yesterday, at 0:20 PM, it is unknown how, but he was careless, and the sparks spread to the sulfur. Suddenly, the wind picked up, and the fire became even fiercer. In an instant, it spread to the neighbors. The neighbors were unable to rescue anything and rushed out to escape and sound the alarm. One person was unable to escape and died in the fire. The fire brigade arrived after hearing the news and extinguished the fire in about an hour. The fire destroyed five or six houses on either side. Later, the fire brigade dug out a corpse from the rubble. The limbs had been charred, and the head and limbs were broken and incomplete. The intestines flowed out of the abdomen, a terrible sight. The body was sent to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch for an autopsy, and the court will be requested to inspect it today. The police station sent detectives to investigate and arrest the arsonist, who is said to have fled. After the incident, it was discovered that a female worker, Duan, 32 years old, from Huzhou, resident of No. 1 Yongkang Lane, Fangbang Road, was missing. It is unknown if she was the person who was burned to death. After an hour and a half, the seventeen rooms in the front, middle, and back buildings were completely destroyed. This can be considered a great disaster for the place.

Total Losses After the fire broke out, because of the bursting of bullets, all the personnel in the office who were enforcing the law and rescuing people, all kinds of case files and important objects in the office, as well as the uniforms and bedding of the police officers, etc., were not able to be taken out. As for the firearms, in addition to the rifles carried by the police officers on duty outside, it is reported that there were still ten rifles, seven Mauser pistols, four pistols, and hundreds of large and small bullets in the office, which were all burned. Fortunately, the police escaped quickly, so no one was injured when the bullets exploded. The total estimated loss is several tens of thousands of gold. As for the detention center in the office, there were no prisoners detained that night, otherwise, due to the danger of flying bullets, they would have had to be released, which would have been too late.

Aftermath Problem A single spark can start a prairie fire.

Fire at Yangjiadu Lights Up Four to Five Li, Public Security Bureau Completely Destroyed 113

Firearms and bullets all burned to ashes

Not a single file or document survived

Fortunately, there were no prisoners in the detention center

A patrol officer's charcoal stove caused a major disaster

The Third District, First Branch of the Pudong Yangjiadu Public Security Bureau suddenly caught fire at 6:45 PM last night. Soon, the fire reached the firearms and bullets, causing explosions, making it impossible to extinguish. As a result, all seventeen rooms of the branch were completely burned down. The details are as follows:

Branch Situation The branch is located on the west side of Yangjiadu Street. It used to be an ancient temple, which was converted into a police station during the Shanghai Police Department era. There are three buildings in the front, middle, and back, facing south. The front building is the dispatch room, detention center, and household registration reporting office. The middle building has a ceremonial hall in the center, the chief's office on the right, and the patrol officer's office and armory on the left. The four temple rooms are the dormitories for the patrol officers. The three rooms in the back are the kitchen and warehouse. Therefore, the area is quite large, and the buildings are very sturdy. As for the surroundings of the branch, the front is the main street, the east and west sides are long alleys, and the west and north sides are vacant land of the Commercial Bureau's new warehouse. Therefore, there are no adjacent buildings on any side.

Sparks Fly Out 114

At 6:45 PM last night, the patrol officer Ouyang Liang lit a charcoal stove in the patrol officer's office to keep warm because the weather was very cold. Unexpectedly, while adjusting the fire, sparks flew out. Patrol Officer Ouyang's bed was covered with straw, and the sparks landed on the straw, causing it to ignite. Patrol Officer Ouyang thought it would be easy to extinguish, but the fire spread to the wallpaper around the room, making it impossible to control. At this time, the chief Yang Zhongquan and the patrol officers rushed over after hearing the alarm. Seeing the patrol officer trying to put out the fire in a confused state, they quickly rescued him. They found that Ouyang's face and hands had been burned. They immediately sounded the alarm whistle for help. In a short while, the fire broke through the roof and spread to the adjacent armory. The bullets of the rifles and pistols were heated by the fire and exploded one after another, flying in all directions. The patrol officers, fearing danger, could not provide any rescue and had to flee. As a result, the fire became more and more uncontrollable.

Difficulty in Rescue 115

The fire was raging, and the red light pierced the sky. Even on a moonlit night, it could be seen from three to five li away. At that time, the north wind was strong, and the fire spread in all directions. The Pudong Fire Brigade heard the alarm and rushed several pump trucks to the scene to put out the fire. However, the location was far from the Huangpu River, and the water in the nearby small river was also scarce, making it difficult to do anything. Before long, the middle and back buildings were completely burned down. The fire was raging, and the front building was also quickly engulfed. The firefighters tried their best to put out the fire with water, but to no avail. After another half hour, the front building was also completely destroyed. At this point, the fire could not be extinguished and gradually diminished, but the interior was still burning fiercely. A total of

Strong Winds and Severe Cold Yesterday, Sea Vessels Were Prevented from Entering the Port 116

Severe cold weather Yesterday, the weather in this port changed drastically. There were strong winds and severe cold, and the temperature dropped to 37 degrees. There was a gale and heavy rain on the sea surface and in the northeast. The climate along the coast of our country and in the Yellow Sea was very bad. There was heavy snow on the Shandong sea. Ningbo Ships Not Operating Yesterday afternoon, all ships at this port received reports from the observatory that there was a strong west wind on the Wenzhou sea. Ningbo-bound ships, such as the China Merchants' Xinjingtian and Sanbei's Ningxing, were suspended. For the sake of safe navigation, the Taikoo's Xinbeijing and Ningshao, two ships operating on the Shanghai-Ningbo route, also stopped exporting yesterday afternoon. Passengers who had boarded the ships all had their tickets refunded and changed to export tomorrow. There will also be no Shanghai-Ningbo ships entering the port today.

Chimney of Fengtai Silk Factory in Zhabei Blown Down by Strong Wind 117

The roof has a very large hole punched through it

Nine people injured, three seriously

At 2:19 PM yesterday, the iron chimney of the Fengtai Silk Factory in Zhabei was suddenly blown down by a strong wind, punching through the roof and injuring many people. Nine people were sent to the hospital. The details are as follows:

Factory Site Survey The Fengtai Silk Factory has been operating for many years, managed by Sun Xianbin (zi Rongchang). It is located between Pingjiang Bridge and Dayang Bridge on the west side, built along the Tanzi River, covering an area of more than ten mu. The main gate faces west. The buildings are very sturdy, all built with forty-inch bricks. There are two floors, with more than 600 male and female workers, mostly female workers.

Incident Situation At 2:15 PM yesterday, when the female workers in the silk reeling workshop upstairs were working, amidst the roar of the northwest wind, they suddenly heard a crashing sound. More than 600 male and female workers were all terrified. A hole about two or three zhang in circumference had been punched through the roof of the silk reeling workshop. Tiles, wooden boards, and other debris fell in a chaotic manner. The workers rushed to escape. Fortunately, the workshop had four wide sluice gates and ladders, and no one was trampled and injured. However, in the area where the accident occurred in the workshop, from No. 140 to No. 154, many people were injured, some in the head, some in the hands and feet, and some in the back.

Injured Names After the accident, the factory manager Sun Rongzhang and other employees rushed to the scene. At the same time, Ge Ruiwei, the patrol officer of the Tanziwan branch of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau, and patrol officers Zhang Lingqing and Cao Jinyang also led more than ten police officers to rush to the scene. In addition to letting all the slightly injured workers off work, the more seriously injured were sent to the Longhua Hospital for treatment in the factory manager's own car. There were a total of nine people, all women, mostly teenage girls. Their names are listed as follows: Ni Xiaohua, Sun Cuinan, Sun Wu, Li Yindi, Xu Wang, Sun Caizhen, Nie Hu, Li Wang, Cao Zhu. Among them, Sun Caizhen, Li Wang, and Nie Hu were the most seriously injured.

Post-Incident Observation At about 4 PM, after hearing the news, the reporter drove to observe the scene. He handed his card to the factory manager Sun Rongchang, inquired about the above situation, and was then led by Sun to observe the various locations. He saw that the chimney was made of five-tenths-inch thick steel plates, with a total of twenty-seven sections, about five or six zhang high, and four chi two cun in diameter. It was secured on all sides with iron cables. However, the wind was too strong, causing the disaster. According to Sun, if the buildings had not been sturdy, the disaster would have been even more severe. Although many people were injured this time, there should be no danger to life, which is considered fortunate. However, the loss of repair costs is very large, and it will take about a week to restore to the original state.

The body burned to death cannot be identified. The gender must be determined after an examination today.

Xi Chunqiao, a Partner of Dalun, Mistakenly Kidnapped 118

▲ Monthly income of only ten yuan

▲ Very poor economy

Xi Chunqiao, a partner of Dalun Silk and Satin Store, was kidnapped on the 9th of this month while traveling from Suzhou to Dongting Dongshan on the Yutai Ferry. In fact, Xi is very poor and works as a low-level clerk, an ordinary merchant. The kidnappers mistakenly thought that Xi was rich and kidnapped him without further investigation. Xi Chunqiao is already 61 years old. He used to work at the Yuanchang Silk and Satin Store in the city and later worked at the Jiuhe Silk and Satin Store. He resigned due to old age and was recommended by a friend to work at Da with a salary of more than ten yuan. He has only an old wife at home and no children. His daily economy is very poor. However, he is honest and has never made any mistakes in more than forty years. Only because he stutters, he could not explain clearly when he was kidnapped. Therefore, the kidnappers saw that he looked tall and burly, and he also had some money that he was carrying home for a fellow villager, so they did not ask about his background and kidnapped him suddenly. It was a misunderstanding.

Ningbo Fellow Association Responds to the Yin County Government, Expressing Opinions on Clearing Sand Fields 119

The Ningbo Fellow Association in Shanghai believes that the former Ningbo Sand Field Branch's handling of the Yin County sand fields has violated the law and disturbed the people, arousing resentment from the victimized owners. Although the Zhejiang Provincial Government has proposed remedial measures, many of them are excessive and deviate from the facts, failing to effectively correct the situation and suppressing public opinion. Yesterday, they specifically raised their opinions and sent a letter to the Yin County Government, requesting them to vigorously preside over the matter. The letter stated: "Upon receiving your letter and the attached Civil Affairs Department's clearance of sand fields to remedy the situation and resolve the various methods, we immediately invited fellow villagers to the association to view them. Everyone believes that the methods proposed by the Civil Affairs Department are excessively biased towards the facts, ignoring the detailed regulations of the Ministry, which is not what a country ruled by law should do. The Sand Field Branch has regulations to follow, but it should follow them but does not, often using approved special cases as an excuse, which is an undeniable violation of the law and oppression of the people. Now, after consultation with the fellow villagers, we propose the following opinions: 1. In the future, the various detailed regulations for clearing sand fields in Zhejiang issued by the Ministry must be strictly followed by the county bureau, and no special cases should be used to make the people have nowhere to turn. 2. When handling , the county bureau should still follow the procedures stipulated by the Ministry and conduct on-site inspections. 3. All cases that have been because the branch has not followed the legal procedures should be announced as invalid." For this matter, we ask Your Excellency, the County Magistrate, to vigorously preside over it, so as to uphold the law and resolve disputes. It is also reported that the owners being tried will organize a Property Rights Protection Committee in Shanghai to handle the registration procedures for victimized owners and vow to oppose the illegal actions of the Sand Field Branch.

Inspection Reports of Two Banks 124

▲Central Bank: The 145th inspection report on the issuance reserve of the Central Bank states: "In accordance with Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this council is responsible for inspecting the reserve for the issuance of convertible banknotes of the bank. On December 10, 1932, Wang Yihou was appointed to conduct the 145th inspection at the Issuance Bureau of the bank. The inspection results are hereby announced as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 35,918,111 silver dollars, including 32,234,165 silver dollar notes and 3,683,946 subsidiary currency notes. Total amount of convertible banknote reserve: 35,918,111 silver dollars, including 29,320,000 silver dollars in cash reserve at the bank, 1,799,918 silver dollars deposited in branches in various cities, 1,844,746 silver dollars deposited in correspondent banks, and 6,589,000 silver dollars in collateral reserve (converted into silver dollars). (B) Total amount of customs gold convertible banknotes issued: 425,000 customs gold units. Total amount of customs gold convertible banknote reserve: 425,000 customs gold units. This reserve includes US$170,000 deposited in this city, valued at 4 units per 425,000 customs gold units. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Banknote Regulations, the cash reserve should be 60% and the collateral reserve should be 40%. This inspection found that the cash reserve exceeded 60% and the collateral reserve was less than 40%. This report is specifically made in accordance with the regulations. December 10, 1932, Central Bank Board of Directors."

▲China Industrial Bank: The issuance department reserve and the business department funds of the China Industrial Bank are completely separate, and the reserve is fully adequate. The issuance reserve figures as of December 10, 1932, are hereby announced as follows: Total amount of convertible banknotes issued: 25,874,601 yuan, including 17,010,340 yuan issued by the bank, 5,181,200 yuan issued by correspondent banks, and 3,490,000 yuan received by various firms. Except for the portions received by various firms, which were inspected according to the original inspection method, this inspection found that the total amount of convertible banknotes issued by the bank was 22,384,601 yuan, and the amount of convertible banknote reserve of the bank was 22,384,601 yuan, including 13,621,601 yuan in cash reserve and 8,762,000 yuan in collateral reserve. The cash reserve accounted for over 60%, and the collateral reserve accounted for under 40%. Both items have been fully and accurately inspected by the inspector, Zhengze Accounting Firm, and accountant Xie Lin.

Turning a Small Matter into a Big Issue: A Meaningless Dispute Between Friends 127

A dispute arising from neon lights and automobiles

Chen Wentao and Cao Yuanfeng become enemies

Friends unsuccessfully attempt to mediate at Y品香

Going to the police station in the middle of the night to confront each other, and even resolving it in court

丨Cao Yuanfeng is acquitted for speaking irresponsibly while drunk丨

Chen Wentao, a salesman for the Xingguang Electric Automobile Advertising Company at the intersection of Fuzhou Road and Jiangxi Road, had recently secured a deal with the Nanjing Hotel to install neon lights made of red and green glass tubes, priced at 3,703 taels of silver. The hotel paid a large portion of the price in cash, with the remaining 1,202 taels to be paid with a promissory note due on November 15th. When the due date arrived, Chen Wentao presented the note for payment. However, Chen's colleague, Cao Yuanfeng, had previously purchased a car from the hotel manager for 900 yuan, paying only 300 yuan and still owing 600 yuan. Cao had not repaid this debt. Therefore, the hotel wanted to deduct the amount owed by Cao from the payment to Chen. Lu Jian resolutely refused. Last Saturday afternoon at 4:00 PM, Chen and Cao negotiated at Xingguang because of this financial entanglement, with Chen claiming that Cao's overdue car payment had made it difficult for him to receive his payment. During the discussion, Chen's anger was visible, and the two sides started arguing and then wrestling. The colleagues tried their best to mediate, and the two sides reluctantly retreated, each with minor injuries. B Zhiying and Li Dayu, intervened as mediators and invited both Chen and Cao to a room at the Y品香 Hotel that evening, hoping that the two would be able to resolve their grievances face-to-face. Although Chen responded to the invitation, Cao could not be found anywhere. The group waited until midnight, but Cao still did not appear, so everyone dispersed. Chen also returned to his home at 193 Qingyu Lane, Dagu Road. However, as he approached the entrance of Qingyu Lane, he saw car number 3838 parked there. Chen knew that the car belonged to Cao. At that moment, seeing the car reminded him of the man, and he suspected that Cao was still angry about what happened during the day and had come to provoke him. Therefore, he dared not go home immediately. Coincidentally, two Chinese constables were on guard at numbers 2203 and 1044 near the alley entrance. Chen told them what had happened and asked them to accompany him home to avoid being harassed by Cao. Both constables agreed. However, when they arrived at his home, Cao was not there. Chen asked his family, and they all said that Cao had not come. Chen then relaxed and went to bed. Unexpectedly, just as he was deep in a sweet dream, the head of the Xinzha police station, Zhao Rongsheng, and the Western inspector, Mr. Wilcocks, arrived at his house, woke Chen up, and summoned him to the police station for questioning. It turned out that after Cao Yuanfeng was persuaded to stop fighting by B and Li, he had no way to vent his anger. He harbored it in his heart until late at night. Not only could he not calm his anger, but he also thought about Chen's job, which had been recommended by Cao himself. Now Chen was publicly disrespecting him, repaying kindness with ingratitude. Who could tolerate this? So he drove to Chen's house, intending to reason with him. However, when he arrived at the door, Chen had not yet returned from Y品香, and Chen's wife refused to open the door late at night, so he returned in vain. On the way, he was almost taken advantage of by petty thieves. Cao became even more suspicious that Chen had plotted against him. Therefore, he reported to the police station, saying that as he was walking out of Qingyu Lane, there was no light in the alley. He only saw three dark figures following closely behind him. Suddenly, he was struck on the head twice with a metal object. He fell down in pain, and when he got up, the dark figures had disappeared. Cao was certain that Chen had a handgun, so he did not dare to chase after them. The police chief felt that the matter was extremely strange and could not believe it. However, Cao firmly insisted that what he encountered was the truth, and he resolutely signed his name on the written record, indicating that if he made a false accusation, he would willingly accept the consequences. When the Chinese and Western detectives brought Chen in for questioning and investigated, it was proven that Chen was still at Y品香 at the time. Cao was then enlightened. Chen also declared that he had a handgun because he was a special constable number 725, but he had surrendered the gun to the police department on the 15th of last month. Cao's report about the handgun was also a lie. The police chief immediately ordered Cao to be detained. Yesterday morning, Cao was handed over to the First Special District Court, where Judge Wu Yanqi questioned him. The police lawyer, Wang Yaotang, explained the case, stating that Cao had indeed violated Article 180 of the Criminal Code, the crime of false accusation. However, after the investigation was clarified, Cao admitted that he had spoken irresponsibly while drunk, which could be excused. He requested the court to consider this. The defendant hired lawyer Jiang Yiping to defend him. Chen Wentao also hired lawyer Zhang Jiahui, stating that he was falsely accused for no reason and that Chen should file a private lawsuit to seek compensation for reputational damages. After Judge Wu questioned both parties and witness B Zhiying, he ruled that the defendant was acquitted.

Reader's Advisory 128

Mr. Zhou Xuegen asks: "I feel that my current job is completely incompatible with my personality. My aversion to my current job is not because I am vain, accustomed to luxury, unwilling to endure hardship, and only want to earn a high salary and achieve a superior position. I just feel that the business I work for is full of feudal colors, extremely conservative, and has no progress at all. The hiring standards only value age, not talent. The entire fate is already entering the abyss of decline. I have no hope for my future. Therefore, I feel that I must find another way out. Although I have an aversion to my current job, I will continue to serve until I get a suitable job. On the one hand, I continue to study hard in my spare time, preparing for the opportunity to come in the future, so that I can abandon the job that is not suitable for my personality and take the job that is suitable for my personality. I am planning like this, please ask whether it is appropriate or not?" Reply: "From your letter, I can know that you have a considerable understanding and considerable insights into the current society, and you are also a young man with vigor and ambition. On this point alone, I can conclude that your future must be bright. We fully agree with your plan. We believe that as long as a person is willing to work hard, there is no problem that cannot be solved. With knowledge, you never have to worry about not having a use for it. However, your efforts should not be solely for the 'individual', but also remember the entire 'society' at all times."

Mr. Zhu Mingchun asks: "My friend, Mr. Chen, is already engaged."

"His fiancée dropped out of school halfway through. Chen asked his parents-in-law to allow her to continue her studies, but his parents-in-law refused and instead became resentful towards Chen. Chen is very disappointed and feels that his fiancée's personality is incompatible with his own. She also cannot manage household affairs. He is considering dissolving the engagement. However, Chen has a job that was introduced by his father-in-law. If he proposes to dissolve the engagement, he is afraid that he will be criticized for being ungrateful. If he does not dissolve the engagement, the future happiness of Chen and his fiancée will be hindered. Is there a better way to resolve this?"

Reply: "Knowing that the other party's 'personality is incompatible with one's own' and still getting engaged is already a mistake. If what is stated in the letter is true, then there are only two options: dissolve the engagement or not. Apart from this, there is no better way to have both. Regarding the problem of Chen's fiancée's schooling, other methods can still be used, such as entrusting someone to discuss it. If Chen feels that his fiancée's personality is fundamentally incompatible with his own, then there is really no way to force it. The marriage issue is of great importance to personal happiness and cannot be used as an exchange item for other conditions. Chen only needs to ask whether dissolving the engagement is 'appropriate' or 'inappropriate'. The unreasonable criticism from society is completely irrelevant." Mr. Lu Xianglin asks: "I have been an apprentice mechanic for two years. Now, due to the shutdown of the factory, I will have to find another job to make a living. Should I continue to learn to be a mechanic? Or should I abandon my original goal and choose another occupation?" "It seems that what the letter says, there is still some hope in entrusting relatives and friends. It's just a matter of 'time'. Since it is impossible to wait passively, it is necessary to think of other methods. But thinking of other methods does not absolutely mean abandoning the mechanic profession. You may as well regard the mechanic profession as your ideal and as the standard for choosing a career. If you can find a mechanic position, then jobs that are similar in nature to the mechanic profession are also possible. If you can't do it again, then temporarily take other professions with different natures, and pay attention to it at any time in the future."

Mr. Qiu Peiliang asks: (1) How to read books? (2) The shopkeeper oppresses me, and my actions are not free. Is there a way to solve it?

Reply: "Regarding the questions in your letter, I will answer them in two points: (1) Most of the current popular publications or books use symbol punctuation, but you still inevitably 'break sentences when reading'. This may be because what you are reading is too deep, or you have not deeply understood each word in a sentence. This is also 'speaking white words' (saying should be 'profession'). You should now first read things that you can understand and simple words slowly. Don't be impatient. If there are words you don't know or don't understand, you should look them up in the dictionary and make sure you understand every word and sentence. Over time, you will naturally see results. (2) The oppression of shop assistants by professional shopkeepers is a common phenomenon in today's society. This is a complete social problem. It is impossible to solve it alone. Now, on the one hand, you can try to improve yourself within the scope of not hindering your work, in order to cultivate your own skills. On the other hand, you can pay attention to opportunities and look for another job."

Xiang Junying asks: "A and B are competing for a piece of land. The land definitely belongs to B, but A knowingly occupies it without any deeds. How will this case be judged?"

Reply: "The trial focuses on evidence. If there is no contract, there should be other evidence, such as human witnesses, boundary stones, various registration certificates, etc. Anything that can prove that the land definitely belongs to B can be presented."

Education News Highlights

Collection of Arrears from Jiangsu Provincial Social Education Institutions 129

The Jiangsu Provincial Social Education Institutions and Teachers' Association held a second joint meeting at the Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang Public Education Center on the afternoon of the 10th of this month at 3:00 PM. Attendees included Yuan Zongze (Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang Sports Field), Zuo Jieru (Provincial Education Department), Wu Zhaochun (Provincial Central Public Education Center), Gan Yuyuan (Jiangsu Provincial Educational Institute), Fan Yongxiang (Jiangsu Provincial Nanjing Public Education Center), Zhu Yunsheng (Jiangsu Provincial Zhenjiang Public Education Center), Kong Yuqing (Jiangsu Provincial Xuzhou Public Education Center), and the Jiangsu Provincial National Studies Library (representative). Zhu Yunsheng presided as chairman, and Gan Yuyuan served as the recorder. The important resolutions made were as follows: (1) The province's education fees have been in arrears for several months, making it difficult for various education institutions to maintain their current operations. Regarding how to solicit payment, the following measures were resolved: 1. A representative group of eight institutions, including Jing Tang Zhenxi, was selected to formally request payment from the Education Fee Management Office, limiting the payment to be made before the end of January of the 12th year, clearing the operating expenses for November of the current year. 2. The representatives of the above-mentioned institutions will gather at the Jingmin Education Center at 2:00 PM on December 14th to go to the management office together. 3. If negotiations fail, they will take concerted action with representatives of primary and secondary schools on the 16th. 4. It is stipulated that the management office must issue expenses to the social education institutions simultaneously with the Jiangsu Provincial Experimental Primary School and the affiliated primary school. (2) The province's social education institutions' staff and teachers' treatment standards and the eligibility criteria for tenure, seniority pay, pension, and bereavement compensation are currently not clearly defined. Regarding whether the association should submit opinions for the department's reference, it was resolved that the director Zeng would separately send letters to each member to draft methods to be submitted to the board of directors for collation before the end of January of the 22nd year for the department's reference. (3) Regarding the proposal to temporarily suspend the payment of income tax because the treatment of the province's social education institutions' staff and teachers cannot be improved, it was resolved that: 1. The association will send a circular to the heads of each institution asking them to temporarily withhold the deducted and unremitted amounts and return the remitted amounts. 2. The association will send a circular to inform the staff and teachers' associations of each institution that after the association's constitution is amended, the Educational Institute, the Jiangsu Provincial Yinzhou Public Education Center, and the Sports Field will be elected as directors of the next joint association.

After the Dissolution of Shandong High School 130

Screening Completed, Classes Resume on January 10th

A communication from Hainan states that the Shandong Provincial High School, which was dissolved by the Education Department on the 5th of this month due to the major unrest caused by opposing the joint entrance examination, has come to an end. As the weather is getting colder and the winter vacation is approaching, the Education Department has ordered the principal, Song Wu, to expedite the handling of the aftermath, which is now largely complete. According to Education Department Director He Siyuan, the high school is approved to resume classes on January 10th. The school will hold a school affairs meeting in the coming days to conduct student screening, and will resume classes immediately after the screening is completed. The missed classes and wasted time of the students this year will be compensated by extending the winter vacation next year. I plan to make a trip to Beijing around the time the high school starts to meet with Education Minister Zhu Jiahua to report on the province's disturbances. As for the city's schools, the winter vacation is scheduled to begin on the 18th of this month.

Junior High School Curriculum Standards (4) 131

Group A is further divided according to individual circumstances, grouping those with similar defects together.

Groups B and C can be further divided according to age, height, and weight.

Group D can select various elective subjects according to the students' interests, such as martial arts competitions, sports, skill selection, dance, etc., and then be divided into groups.

Note: If classes are held in groups according to this example, attention must be paid to the timetable. It is best to dedicate the time after 2:00 PM every day to physical education and not schedule other classes.

(Example 2) According to the Cao Tong grade system:

First step: Divide each class into male and female groups.

Second step: Divide each class according to the physical examination results. Those who need special corrective exercises are separated into one group, and the rest are divided into several groups according to age, height, physical fitness, or skills. They still attend classes in the same class but use grouped teaching methods. Each group is set up with a group leader to assist the teachers in taking responsibility for order and leadership. The teachers must provide additional guidance and teaching to the group leaders.

(Example 3) A reconciliation method of the above two. Teaching time according to Example (2).

Hygiene 132

First, Objectives

(1) To enable students to understand the correct meaning of hygiene.

(2) To cultivate hygienic habits to enhance their physical and mental health. (3) To enable students to increase their interest and confidence in daily hygiene, with the hope that individual efforts will promote the health of families, schools, and the social environment. (4) To enable students to understand the structure and physiology of the human body, as well as methods for health maintenance and disease prevention.

(5) To enable students to have a basic understanding of simple methods for nursing and first aid.

Second, Time Allocation

(1) Regular class, lectures and experiments: one hour per week, taught for a total of three academic years.

(2) The practice of hygienic habits is included in the usual grades.

(3) Extracurricular assignments, same as above.

Third, Teaching Material Outline

(1) First Academic Year (Human Anatomy, Physiology, and Health)

(1) General introduction to personality, 1. Skeleton and posture, 2. Structure of various organ systems, 3. Weight and height, (2) Muscles and nerves, (3) Nervous system and mental health, (4) Respiration, (5) Blood and blood circulation, (6) Nutrition 1. Digestive organs, 2. Elements of nutrition, 3. Food selection, 4. Food digestion, 5. Metabolism, 6. Excretion, 7. Body temperature, 8. Elements of development, (7) Endocrine, (8) Mouth, teeth, eyes, ears, (9) Physiological changes during puberty, (10) Exercise physiology, (11) Harm of tobacco and alcohol, (12) Meaning of health.

(1) Second Academic Year (Common Knowledge of Diseases)

(1) Health and disease, 1. Meaning of disease, 2. Discovery of pathogens, 3. Death and autopsy, (2) Classification of diseases, 1. Classification based on age, 2. Classification based on pathology, A. Heredity, B. Malformation, C. Inflammation, 1. Nutritional deficiencies, E. Degeneration, F. Accidents, (3) Human parasites, (4) Diseases of animals (livestock, etc.) and their relationship, (5) Bacteria, immunity, and disinfection, (6) Infectious diseases 1. Definition, A. Infectious diseases, B. Endemic, epidemic, pandemic, C. Vehicles of transmission, D. Carriers of pathogens, E. Unrecognized diseases, 2. Principles of human infection of infectious diseases, A. Resistance, susceptibility, immunity, etc. of the host, B. Pathogens, virulence, quantity, transmission routes, etc., C. Environmental factors, climate, season, sanitation, etc., 3. Epidemic infectious diseases (focus on symptoms and prevention), A. Typhoid fever (enteric fever), B. Cholera, C. Dysentery, D. Smallpox (with vaccination techniques), E. Diphtheria, F. Scarlet fever, G. Measles, H. Meningococcal meningitis, I. Whooping cough, J. Chickenpox, K. Others, (4) E. The problem of tuberculosis in our country, (5) Venereal diseases, A. Pathogen, B. Transmission, C. Pathology, D. Treatment, E. The problem of venereal diseases in our country, 6. Leprosy, 7. Trachoma, 8. Skin diseases (scabies, ringworm), 9. Rabies, 10. Plague.

(3) Third Academic Year (Public Health)

(1) History of medicine and public health development, 1. The era of divine authority, 2. The scientific era, (2) Environmental hygiene, 1. Water, 2. Feces and garbage, 3. Sewage system, 4. Housing, 5. Supervision of food and beverages (slaughterhouses, vegetable markets, restaurants, etc.) 6. Eradication of flies, lice, rats, etc., (3) Prevention of infectious diseases, 1. Procedures for managing infectious diseases (reporting, investigation, isolation, disinfection, etc.), 2. Vaccination, 3. Quarantine of vehicles and ships, (4) Maternal and child health, 1. Causes and prevention of maternal mortality, 2. Causes and prevention of infant mortality, 3. Health care for preschool children, (5) School hygiene, 1. School environmental hygiene, 2. Health check-ups and correction of deformities, 3. Prevention of infectious diseases in schools, 4. Physical training, 5. Health education, (6) Occupational hygiene, (7) Urban safety design, 1. Disaster prevention, 2. Transportation, 3. Entertainment venues, 4. Others, (8) Harm of proprietary medicines, (9) Current status of national health in our country, and the relationship between the need for health education and socio-economic factors, (10) Organization of public health administration, 1. International, 2. National, 3. Provincial, 4. Central, 5. County and rural areas, 6. Current status of public health administration in our country, (11) Simple first aid methods, 1. Bandages, 2. Bleeding and hemostasis methods, 3. Trauma, A. Wounds, B. Burns, C. Frostbite and chilblains, D. Fractures, dislocations, and sprains, 4. Drowning, suffocation, strangulation, and artificial respiration, 5. Fainting, sunstroke, 6. Poisoning, A. Coal gas, B. Opium, C. Arsenic, 7. First aid for common ailments, with application of first aid medicines and materials (schools, families, factories).

Fourth, General Implementation Methods

(1) Work Items

(1) Regular class, 1. Experiments and demonstrations of necessary hygiene and physiological matters, 2. Practice various first aid methods, 3. Read and describe books on hygiene, 4. Produce hygiene thesis reports and charts.

(2) Practice of hygienic habits

(3) Extracurricular assignments, 1. Implement health check-ups, 2. Individually correct students' physical illnesses and shortcomings in autonomous hygiene, 3. Implement vaccinations for smallpox, typhoid fever, cholera, scarlet fever, diphtheria, etc., 4. Inspect the hygienic conditions of school buildings and internal facilities, 5. Investigate the public health conditions of society, 6. Conduct Cleanliness Movement Week, Fly Eradication Movement Week, Mosquito Eradication Movement Week, etc., 7. Write hygiene propaganda materials, 8. Hold regular hygiene lectures, 9. Hold performances of hygiene operas and talks of hygiene stories, 10. Visit various hygiene medical institutions.

(2) Teaching Method Key Points

(1) Teachers themselves should practice hygienic habits and pay attention to health, setting an example.

(2) The teaching material outline above only indicates the scope of research; its organizational methods can be adjusted according to various circumstances.

(3) Use everyday life issues as a starting point for discussion, gradually moving towards a scientific study of personal, family, social, and environmental hygiene.

(4) Take advantage of opportunities to implement designed teaching, and should pay attention to observation, experimentation, demonstration, discussion, etc.

(5) Operations outside the classroom should be mutually connected, and should be guided and assisted.

(6) Grade assessment should focus on students' daily healthy behaviors.

(7) Connect with other sciences.

(8) Conduct regular health check-ups; if there are diseases and defects, try to correct them.

(9) Organize health groups, practice various hygienic habits under the guidance of teachers and staff, and implement first aid.

(10) Fully prepare models, charts, specimens, instruments, etc. necessary for teaching, so that students have a concrete understanding and practice.

(11) Try to set up medical and nursing clinics, and implement preventive injections, etc., so that students practice and know the necessary conditions for health.

▲ 18th of this month

County Rural Teachers' and Students' Permanent Patriotic Donation 136

The teachers and students of the County Rural Normal School, in light of the fact that the Northeast Volunteer Army is fighting hard in the ice and snow without assistance, suffering from hunger and cold, decided through a faculty meeting that teachers would deduct 1% of their monthly salary, and students would donate one copper coin per month, starting immediately and remitting monthly to the Northeast, as a permanent patriotic donation.

Teng Junfu Visits Patriotic Girls' School to Give a Speech 137

Teng Junfu, a preparatory member of the China Boy Scouts General Association and a representative of the current session, arrived in Shanghai to attend the unveiling ceremony of the Monument to Martyred Boy Scouts in this city. Yesterday, he visited the Patriotic Girls' School and paid particular attention to the Girls Scouts training class. The school held a special meeting to welcome him. Mr. Teng gave a speech on the mission of women in the future, emphasizing the importance of spiritual liberation, stating that modern women must have adequate knowledge, noble personality, and strong physical bodies. He recognized the school's historical position and hoped that all students would prepare in time to lead the liberation of women in the future. Xu Guanchu, Jiang Wushi, and others then gave speeches in succession.

Outstanding Literary Works by Jinan University Students Published 139

Kong Jiajun, a student in the Department of Chinese Literature at Jinan University, due to the emotional ties with Fu Xia, used his great writing power to transform his distant feelings and deep hatred into poetry, named the "Nai He Collection." The entire collection is well-structured and can be read as a poem or a novel. Each piece is filled with a sense of the times and is elegantly written, excelling in the styles of Chu Ci, Yuefu, Ci, and Qu. Tao Pu An inscribed a poem, praising it as "bamboo slips and wind robes, talent is determined," and also saying "casting poems into a new style, who says there are no extraordinary texts today." Chen Zhongfan's comments stated, "tender and poignant, no love poem in ancient times has been written like this." In addition, there are prefaces by President Zheng Hongnian, old poet Chen Shiyi, Hu Huaichen, and Zhao Jingchen. The book is signed "Gufan," uses a Song-style font, Haiyue paper, and a new-style layout, making it exceptionally exquisite. Beixin is the general distributor, and bookstores such as the Author, New Moon, Shenzhou, China, and Wenhua are agents for sale. The price is one yuan, with a 20% discount.

Implementation of the National Physical Education Implementation Plan Guangdong Province Holds Mass Sports Experiment Area The Provincial Affairs Meeting Approved an Opening Fee of 3,000 Yuan 142

The experiment area includes Guangzhou City and Panyu County.

Recently, in the midst of national crisis, it is not enough for the people of the whole country to rise up to save the country. Although there is an indomitable spirit, it is still necessary to have a strong physique to fight a long-term defense against insults. Therefore, the popularization of mass education is an urgent task today. The Guangdong Provincial Department of Education specially ordered the Department of Education to issue the "National Physical Education Implementation Plan" and stipulated that a Guangdong Provincial Mass Sports Experiment Area should be established, with a term tentatively set at two years. In the future, the effective methods of the experiment area will be extended to all counties and cities in the province to promote the initial stage of mass education. The Guangdong Provincial Mass Sports Experiment Area Implementation Outline was immediately drafted and submitted to the Provincial Affairs Meeting on the 6th of this month. It was resolved that the opening fee for the experiment area would be 3,000 yuan, and the monthly recurring expenses would be 750 yuan. The opening fee and the recurring expenses for each month from December of this year to June of next year would be temporarily allocated from the 21st year education temporary fee item, and from July of the 22nd year, they would be included in the annual budget for expenditure. The contents of the Guangdong Provincial Mass Sports Experiment Area Method are as follows: Article 1: This experiment area aims to promote mass sports groups by implementing the National Physical Education Implementation Plan. Article 2: The actual name is Guangdong Provincial Mass Sports Experiment. Article 3: The site of this experiment area is temporarily located in the Guangdong Provincial Public Sports Field on Dadong Road, Guangzhou City, with Guangzhou City and Panyu County as the experiment area. Article 4: The experimental period is tentatively set at two years, starting from the 23rd year, and the methods implemented by the experimental area will be popularized to all departments in the province. Article 5: The administrative personnel of the experiment area are as follows: A. One area director, who presides over all affairs of the area; one deputy director, who assists the director in handling all affairs of the area. (B) One sports instructor from the Municipal Education Bureau, who assists in the affairs of the area. (C) A specially appointed staff member from the Provincial Mass Education Personnel Training Institute. (D) A specially appointed staff member from the Provincial Mass Education Hall. (E) One member of the Guangdong Provincial Sports Committee. (F) One specially appointed area teacher, and one to five hired staff members. Article 6: Those with original duties among the staff of this area will not be paid separately, but may be appropriately paid for expenses incurred on official business. Article 7: The experiment area is divided into sports, health, propaganda, and general affairs sections. The administrative system is as follows:

丨Sports Section丨Staff

丨Health Section

Department of Education Fourth Section丨Director Deputy 丨Director Deputy Propaganda Section

丨General Affairs Section

丨Specially Appointed Teacher

Article 8: The undertakings undertaken by the experiment area are as follows: A. Hold two to four mass amateur sports meetings each year. B. Hold various types of track and field events. C. Organize national martial arts classes (such as Chinese new-style martial arts and Tai Chi exercises, etc., all those that conform to scientific methods of educational principles can be adopted). 丨Organize various fitness groups (such as organizing morning exercises for businessmen when businessmen have time). E. Conduct mobile sports and national martial arts guidance. F. Separately hold health competitions for adult men and women each year. G. Sports lectures, H. Sports posters, I. Sports exhibitions, J. Sports publications. Article 9: The annual expenses of this experiment area will be paid by the provincial department during the experiment period. After popularization, they will be paid by the Education Bureau and included in the budget. (December 6th evening)

Huilan had good coordination, but their shooting was not accurate. In the first half, Shanghai High School won with a score of 14 to 8. In the second half, Huilan's performance declined sharply, and their offense and defense were poor. Shanghai High School's score increased steadily, and they won with a score of 47 to 19. Shanghai High School thus obtained the final right.

Research on Football Tactics (II) 147

Written due to the first defeat of the Batavia Qunli Team

After the football match that day, on the way home, a passionate supporter of Qunli said to me angrily, constantly blaming the other team members for not providing adequate support and ruining a winnable situation. In his overreaction, he even said that the Qunli were all useless people, and that his anger had reached boiling point, which is why he said such things. However, impartially speaking, apart from Adek Wu, there are probably no other truly outstanding players in Qunli. They do not have a thorough understanding of the science of football. Their practice sessions seem decent in terms of footwork and ball control, but once they are in a real match (especially after conceding a goal), they completely lose their normal control and instinct to manage the ball in a rush or in a state of over-anxiety. This is because

there is no good evidence of having experienced big matches, and the players invariably suffer from stage fright. To get rid of this problem, it is best to work hard on one's own skills, because as the saying goes, "A person with great skill has great courage." In a football match, only those with great skill are courageous and careful; only those who are courageous and careful can take full advantage. In addition, I have also heard that Qunli are always as brave as tigers when they encounter strong teams, performing exceptionally well, but when they encounter weak opponents, they perform poorly and without energy, so they often achieve unexpected feats. It is really unbelievable that Qunli was able to defeat the Chinese-Portuguese team last year, because everyone knows that the overall and individual strength of the Chinese-Portuguese team is much higher than that of Qunli. This kind of inconsistent state is also something that will only be discovered when each individual's skill has not reached perfection. With the old habit of saying what I know, I want to put forward a few points for my teammates to study, and on the one hand, I also hope that they will not think of me as a busybody and can pay a little attention: (1) Get rid of the habit of dribbling. (Dribbling can only be used when absolutely necessary or when one's own side is winning and wants to delay time.) (2) Learn to kick cross balls more often, so that one's kicks can reach where one wants them to go. (3) Passes should have a certain purpose and intention, as well as a considerable degree of accuracy. (Our team gets the ball no small number of times during matches, but after getting the ball, blind kicking is very common, and the effect is equal to nothing, and it also wastes energy. A wise man would not do this.) (4) Practice immediate kicking. (Many teammates have the bad habit of stopping the ball before kicking it. This must be greatly improved.) (5) The left foot is not very flexible. Sometimes, when the ball comes to the left foot, one has to lean the body to the right before one can execute a kick. However, all top-notch players use both left and right feet. Practice until the ball comes from either side and is controlled by that side to save time. Practice until you don't always have to look at the position of the ball when controlling it, but can imagine it in your feeling. Then you can say that you are a good player (6) Header is one of the important parts of the ball game. When topping, you should first observe the direction of the ball and predict the landing point. (7) When it is a few yards away from the landing point, you should make an effort to jump to the highest point that your strength can reach. When topping, do not be afraid of pain, do not shrink your neck, do not bend your waist, and do not bend your legs. Look at the ball with your eyes and concentrate on this top. Focus on the opportunity to respond, either forward or backward or left and right, so that the pass can reach your own team, which is the step that should be taken on the head. Our team's heading needs to be greatly improved. (8) Put the football on the football's freedom, and do more research on the time to distinguish the value of sooner or later (time is the most important point, and the effect is different if you kick the ball early or late. More people in our team think that it is a small thing and ignore it, and they are unwilling to study it, which is really wrong.) (9) Common sense should be learned more often, cut and studied more, and applied more practically. (For example, in the last game, the middle road was blocked, so we should have advanced to the side as soon as possible, and for example, when we lost the first ball at the beginning of the game, it was still early, but we were eager to retaliate and kicked the ball as if we were afraid of not being in a hurry. We lost the standard repeatedly in a hurry, and when we lost the second ball in the last five minutes, there was little time left, so we should have been back to the city. *

Borrow one, use a blitzkrieg to try to win back the draw, but instead take things calmly. When the ball comes to your feet, you take it yourself and are unwilling to release it, which is a mistake.

Think about it, no one can be perfect, and everyone has weaknesses. As long as you can make up your mind and learn from each other's strengths and weaknesses, you will make progress. (10) Be humble and willing to be taught, and do not be ashamed to ask questions. It is not shameful to ask others for advice if you do not understand, but it is really shameful to not understand but think you understand and disdain to ask others. Asking questions and discussing are shortcuts to success. I think that those who play football well do not necessarily have the ability to teach others. On the other hand, those who can teach others are not necessarily football players. It is beneficial to discuss a difficult problem with anyone. For example, I have always liked people to ask questions, although I dare not admit that I am a good teacher, and I dare not say that my own opinions, arguments, strategies and playing styles are the best, but I dare to say that I have been in the football world for more than ten years, and the two items of research and experience have indeed given me unlimited knowledge and the rewards of teaching and training. If you don't abandon me and come and talk about your football experience, I dare to guarantee that you will definitely gain some benefits from the discussion.

The above is only a rough idea. There are also some subtle points that I can't think of for a while, so I would like to ask everyone to use their brains to study them and work hard to improve. Brothers, let's get started. The lush garden of success does not limit who can enter it. As long as you have the desire to enter that beautiful garden, you will eventually reach it. Look, the gatekeeper of the Garden of Success is holding the key and smilingly waiting for you! !! (To be continued)
