Free Talk

Short Story

He Who Steals a Hook is Executed (III) 148

— Zhu Wen

"Hey, hey! Don't run, Little Pockface, catch the thief!" A loud voice shouted behind Dafa. Sande, who was thinking about the things in the basket, was even more frightened than Dafa. He saw clearly that it wasn't shouting at him. His own hands hadn't reached into the basket yet.

The man who was browsing eggplants and green beans near Dafa stood up, and the two big baskets collided as he chased after the person in front.

"Catch this little thief, I turned around and he stole three big eggplants! ...... Hey, Mr. Lao San of the tofu shop, thank you for keeping an eye on my load!"

Those who heard it paid attention to this new excitement.

A child running in front stepped on something and almost slipped, but he ran desperately. There were many people on the road, and the more he wanted to run fast, the more quietly he ran. In the end, he was grabbed by a fat man with a long basket, who looked like a chef in a rich family. The child was as thin as firewood and couldn't withstand the powerful grab. He retreated crookedly for many steps and squatted on the ground. But the big eggplant in his hand was still tightly held and not let go. Just as he got up from the ground, the eggplant seller had already come up to him.

"Why are you stealing my things? I can't earn much money in a day's business. If you steal three, how can I make a living?"

The child had a fierce look on his face. Seeing the eggplant seller coming to snatch the things in his hand, he tried to run away like a madman, but he couldn't escape. He said...

"Just let me eat these three, I don't know how long it's been since I had anything to eat. Just do a good deed."

"If you want to eat, I want to eat too. If everyone comes to steal like you, I won't be able to eat. If you want to eat, you should go to your father. How can you start stealing at such a young age!"

"Then give me some to eat when you have food to eat! My father starved to death, and my mother does odd jobs sewing and can't support both of us. I have nowhere to go to beg for food."

The eggplant seller was stunned when he heard it. The child, like a hungry beast, wanted to rush past the crowd and escape again.

"This little bastard, listen to his nonsense. He's so young and already steals things. If he's not taught a lesson, what will he be like when he grows up?"

The child was angry when he heard this in the crowd. He threw an eggplant at the person, saying...

"It's not stealing yours, what's it to you! If I don't steal, I'll starve to death, you can't control me!"

The eggplant seller was really angry when he saw the child throwing his eggplant.

"Little thief, so it's right for you to steal other people's things?"

The person in the crowd who was hurt by the eggplant took two steps forward angrily and, together with the eggplant seller, raised his fists. The fists fell on the child's body.

"Ah," Dafa was careless for a moment, and when he looked again, the child's mouth was already bleeding.

Seeing the blood seemed to make everyone happy, and the lesson was over. They pushed the child aside, and before they had walked three steps, the child fell down again. The eggplant seller picked up the three eggplants and grumbled back to his own basket. Although he had lost a little,

This way, he would do a few less businesses, but he felt happy in his heart.

"Dafa, let's go, what are you standing there for?"

Dafa turned around and saw Sande holding a few big garlics and a few small radishes in his hands. He was strangely about to ask Dafa, when he suddenly understood everything.

"Aren't you afraid of being beaten! Go to a small alley," Dafa asked anxiously, biting the radish.

"I'm more clever than the child. I also have to thank him, because people are anxious to watch the excitement, so I can start. I took it from a basket of people who bought a lot of big fish and meat. It's not worth eating raw fish and meat, so I'll be polite to him."

A smile appeared on Sande's face.

May 1932, Shanghai.

Is Love Unconditional? 149

— Ms. Zhuo Ji

Unconditional love has become a thing of the past. As for now, most people have admitted that love is not unconditional. Naturally, I am one of the majority.

Although it is generally acknowledged that love has conditions, the conditions vary from person to person. In fact, those who sing the praises of unconditional love have conditions implicitly contained in the essence of their love, but they themselves do not feel it or are unwilling to say it.

What are the conditions of love? People usually think that it is money, power, and beauty. It is no wonder that people misunderstand it like this, because many lovers often take this as a condition now. In fact, besides this, there are many other conditions, such as profound knowledge, noble morality, common thoughts, upward aspirations, strong will, special talents, strong body, appropriate age, gentle temperament, etc. After counting, it is always nothing more than two kinds of ranges: material and spiritual, or external and internal. A person can have one condition or several conditions as her or his standard for choosing a lover.

I dare to say that conditional love does not tarnish the sacredness of love. To judge whether sacred love is tarnished by conditions, one must first see what the conditions of the person who speaks of love are. In other words, only those who take money, power, and beauty as conditions are despicable and vulgar; and those who take knowledge, temperament, body, thought, ambition, talent, etc. as conditions are just, reasonable, and noble. The former's love can be said to be a buy-and-sell type, a pimp and prostitute type, while the latter's love is not. It is mutual love, it is truly pure love. The former is not love at all, it is simply a boring impulse, prone to danger. Either the woman is abandoned, or she has another lover, or she remarries. The latter is not the case. Their love is rationalized and has a deep foundation, so it is lasting and unchanging.

I feel that now that slightly ambitious women who want to be independent often regard marriage as an annoying problem. If they get married, their future will be buried in family life. If they do not get married, they will inevitably suffer the trouble of being pursued and slandered by those whose marriage proposals are not successful. Therefore, between marriage and non-marriage, one must choose one. Which is good? I think it's better not to get married. If you want to get married, you must be careful. Love should be rationalized, that is, to set reasonable and pure conditions to choose your partner, and never be tempted by money or gigolos. A marital relationship combined by such love will not only not make one's ambition decline, but also encourage each other to do what each other should do. Therefore, I advocate that love must have conditions.

"Is love conditional?" This is a practical question and an interesting question. Now this question has been re-raised by Ms. Wei Ji. "Young men" and "beautiful young ladies" who are burning with the fire of love, please consider carefully the questions that are closely related to you, and please make public your brilliant opinions. Performing Arts 151

— Tao

In the Xinwen Bao and Shanghai Chen Bao the day before yesterday, and in yesterday's edition of this newspaper, Mr. Tao Xingzhi published an advertisement for performing arts, selling his writing, calligraphy, and lectures.

His advertisement contained four lines of poetry: "Who dares to unleash Li Kui's fire in these high winds? Even Wu Xun finds begging difficult! Suicide avoids imprisonment, but I'll never play the bowing game." These four lines not only depict an outline of this畸形 society, but also reflect Mr. Tao's entire personality. Unwilling to set fires, finding begging difficult, and suicide being a criminal act, how difficult it is to be a person in contemporary society!

Mr. Tao is an educator with principles. "Teaching, learning, doing" is his slogan. Anyone who has visited Xiaozhuang Normal School or read "Ancient Temple Bell Ringing Record" published in this newspaper will likely not doubt this statement. Therefore, Mr. Tao's writing and lectures are accumulated experience, full of "strength" and "ability." As for his calligraphy, it also possesses a composed strength. Regarding these, although Mr. Tao himself did not loudly proclaim like a melon seller, "How sweet my melons are!" we can prove that Mr. Tao's melons are indeed sweet!

Originally, in our country, everyone understands a little about business. Everything before us is nothing but "business dealings": buying and selling positions, buying and selling favors, buying and selling lives all become legitimate transactions. However, the female student selling her art at the Confucius Temple in Nanjing was expelled for allegedly damaging the school's reputation. From this, we can imagine that selling art is not easy. Precisely because art is not easy to sell, "favors" and "lives" are easy to sell. We do not want this phenomenon to continue, so we greatly approve of Mr. Tao's willingness to "bite the bullet and give it a try."

If society is discerning, I think Mr. Tao will not have to wait until "choosing an auspicious day to open," and will certainly have "a prosperous business!"

Hydroelectric Power 152

— Qiong

People have long known to use the power of nature's water to promote human progress, such as water-powered rice hullers and water-powered mills. In recent centuries, the principles of electricity have been invented, and we have learned to use electromagnetism to generate electricity with mechanical power. Later, we were able to generate electricity from mountain streams. Therefore, in the past fifty or sixty years, humans have worked hard to develop water resources, and now we are at the height of the hydroelectric power era.

But what does a hydroelectric power project look like? First, a dam is built in the river to create a large reservoir upstream. If using lake water, this is naturally not necessary. Second, a water intake is built at a right angle to the river, and sediment or other debris is removed from the water. The water is then channeled through a waterway into a penstock. A penstock is inclined upwards at the water intake and is equipped with a pressure pipe to allow the water to descend rapidly. A water turbine is installed at the lower end of the pressure pipe, which rotates due to the impact of the water force. The water turbine is directly connected to a generator to produce electricity. The electricity then passes through a transformer to increase the voltage and is sent to a substation via power lines. Finally, the voltage is reduced at the substation and transmitted to users' homes.

Economical hydroelectric power plants are of course large-scale and capable of producing large amounts of electricity, but with technological advances and reduced operating costs, even small power plants are very economical. However, small power plants require many workers, so automated power plants that do not use workers are now very developed. There has been significant progress in this area recently.

Automated hydroelectric power plants are divided into two types. One type starts the motor of the automated power plant when the power supply in the main power plant is insufficient or when the main power plant's switch is closed due to necessity, and transmits a corresponding amount of power. The other type is purely automatic. For example, if the water level in the automated power plant's reservoir is completely stable at a certain height but its float continues to rise, the control circuit mechanism is automatically closed and the power plant begins to rotate. When the water level drops, the plant automatically stops and waits for the required water level to be restored.

The Lolo People of Yunnan (2) 153

— Wang Yu

When it was time to drip water, many women and old men would put on clean clothes, fill a gold, silver, or other bottle or pot with clear water, and take it to the Burmese temple. Then, the Great Buddha would lead them in chanting scriptures while dripping the clear water from the bottles, drop by drop, onto the faces of each idol. It is said that this is to show respect to the idols. If they respect you, they will also sprinkle clear water on you.

The Burmese temple is kept exceptionally clean, so the people who live in the temple are often barefoot. No one is allowed to step into the place where the idols are worshiped wearing shoes. If they violate this rule, they will be severely punished.

(3) Their attire is similar to that of the Han Chinese due to their mingling, but in women's fashion, special sentiments are still expressed.

They do not bind their feet like country girls, nor do they constrict their chests like urban misses. In short, their bodies are very healthy. Although they keep long hair, they do not wear it over their shoulders. They wear short white tops and long black skirts. Their skirts are a whole piece of cloth five feet long and three feet wide. They wear a long belt around their waist at the edge of the skirt and tie it very tightly because they regard a slender waist as beautiful. On their heads, they wear headscarves like Indians, but their headscarves are very long. When they wrap them around their heads, it looks like they are wearing straw hats, so the scorching sun cannot tan their fair and tender faces.

In the past, both men and women liked to dye their teeth a lacquer-like black, considering it beautiful. Women also wore a pair of earrings. But now, such decorations can no longer win honor among the Lolo people and have almost disappeared.

They do not like to wear powder or rouge.

(4) Their customs. Speaking of their customs, they are truly interesting. I remember when I was in elementary school, I went with my grandfather to visit a Lolo family. When we sat down, the old host first sat on the left and then invited my grandfather to sit on the right. At that time, my grandfather also liked to pay attention to these vulgar etiquettes, so he rushed to the right side and gave the left seat to the old host. I was a bit confused when I saw this, and when I got home, I told my father, and he explained to me that the Lolo people consider the right side to be larger and the left side to be smaller, which is the opposite of the Han Chinese's custom of considering the left side to be larger and the right side to be smaller.

When we have guests at home, don't we prepare good food and accompany our guests while they eat and drink? But the Lolo people's etiquette is not like this. If the Lolo people treat you as an honored guest, they will set up a table of food for you to enjoy alone. In our eyes, this simply implies an intention to send the guest away, but to them, it is a special hospitality.

(5) Their Entertainment. Every year, ten days before the Qingming Festival, they have a religious form of entertainment called "Picking Flowers," or "Picking Big Flowers." At this time, they stop all work, put on new clothes, and everyone puts on a cheerful face, as if we were celebrating the New Year or Westerners were celebrating Christmas.

They begin this entertainment ten days before Qingming, but they only play the most lively on the tenth day before Qingming, so they call that day "Big Picking," and the previous days are called "Small Picking."

During the small picking, the young monks in the Burmese temple first beat the drums at the entrance of the Burmese temple, strike the gongs, knock the cymbals, and clap the small cymbals commonly used on stage, playing in a simple rhythm for half a day, indicating that the "picking flowers" game has begun. From this time on, many men and women freely gather at the Burmese temple every afternoon, each holding a handful of household flowers or wildflowers, and a pair of bowls -- either wooden bowls, porcelain bowls, or earthen bowls, and sometimes even gold bowls. This pair of bowls is prepared for "taking sand" in the clear stream.

The Crossroads of Era and Love 13 154

— Zhang Ziping

Yao Xing said, imitating the way a woman walks for Haiquan to see, and at the same time making a face. So the two of them laughed in the gloomy empty classroom for a while.

The old janitor cleaning the classroom walked in with a broom. They hurriedly walked out of the classroom.

Today, Tang Yaoxing treated Haiquan to dinner at a Russian restaurant at the intersection of Avenue Joffre and Route Cardinal Mercier, and also talked to him a lot about the recent situation in the literary world. His main point was that China's literary and art circles are really too bad, a mess. As long as you settle on a proposition and work actively, you can definitely dominate the literary world. The reason why the literary and art circles were so bad in the past was that there was no school of thought with a clear proposition.

But Haiquan felt a little uncomfortable when he heard this, and couldn't help but retort to him.

"Didn't Brother Zhou, Brother Jin, and Brother Ma publish a literary magazine with a clear proposition?"

"What does that count for! The first sentence is two lines of tears, and the second sentence is a burst of hot blood. It's simply nonsense! There's no systematic theory at all."

Haiquan couldn't answer for a moment when Yao Xing retorted.

Zhou De, Jin Meishan, and Ma Zhiyu are the founders of the Mars Literary Society, which was recently established. They are promoting the banner of socialist literature and art and have published a new magazine called "Mars Literary Monthly." They are celebrating and cheering, like a newly opened grocery store, inviting a band of Western musicians to play and bang on their building, dinging and donging.

Haiquan thought that Tang Yaoxing's proposition was a bit too strong. Even if what he said was right, his manner of speaking with his neck tilted would really cause the other party to feel disgusted. Even a reasonable proposition would become an unreasonable one.

When they parted, Tang Yaoxing repeatedly urged him to introduce him to Mr. Chen Huamin another day, and asked him to keep it a secret.

When Haiquan took the tram back to Professor Zeng's residence, he heard a lot of noise in the house, as if many people were talking. He felt a little strange, so he stopped and peeked in. But he didn't understand a word, because the people inside were speaking Japanese. He thought there were guests in the front living room, so it was inconvenient to pass through there. He hurried to the back door and knocked, and the maid opened the door. As soon as he stepped in, he heard Mrs. Hezi coming out and standing by the door at the bottom of the stairs.

"Mr. Lin is back? Have you had dinner?"

"I've eaten."

He replied and planned to go upstairs. But curiosity told him to steal a glance into the living room in front. He saw a Japanese man and two Japanese women. The man looked a bit old, at least over forty.

"They just came from the Japanese countryside. Let me entertain them for a while. I'm really sorry, Mr. Lin."

Mrs. Hezi smiled at him with one hand on the banister of the stairs. Her smile was a bit like begging for his pity. Haiquan didn't understand why she wanted to show him that kind of attitude. He just nodded and went straight upstairs.

When Tang Yaoxing asked him to join their literary group, he was seven-tenths willing. However, it was inconvenient to agree immediately and he had to be humble. Thinking that he would have the opportunity to publish his articles in the future, he couldn't help but feel happy again.

New York Stock Market Weakens First, Then Recovers 161

A report from the Xin Feng Foreign Firm: Last Saturday (the 10th), the New York stock market showed a downward trend due to profit-taking at the end of the week. American United stocks were particularly weak, due to the expectation that unfilled orders would decrease. However, due to the strength of the British pound, stable bonds, firm commodities, and an increase in railway freight cars (53,570), the decline in individual stocks was relatively small. The half-day trading volume was 408,000 shares. The Dow Jones index for the 10th is listed below:

Yarn and Cotton Yarn Market Rises Suddenly After Prolonged Slump 162

丨Large Clearance of Spot Yarn丨

The long-depressed yarn market has suddenly surged. As harmful currency becomes more active and the cotton market remains firm, the yarn market has been further elevated. Fellow traders are mostly empty-handed and without goods. The demeanor of customer groups shows vitality, and their mindset has suddenly changed, leading to vigorous market searching. Many believe that the base is small and there is some interest in going long. The future depends on real sales.

Bidding Becomes More Intense The market opening was tight. Good news was heard from customer groups regarding spot yarn. There was a lack of sellers in the market. Recent months rose by 1.12 taels, and distant months rose by 0.07 to 0.09 taels. In the afternoon, domestic Sichuan gangs bought a great deal of spot goods, resulting in a very brisk situation. The buying trend became more intense. However, large short positions remained unchanged.

Cotton Market Rises Sharply 164

▲Arrivals Scarce丨Prices in Production Areas Higher Than in Shanghai▲

The rise in the cotton market is intensifying, but overseas cotton markets are showing mixed trends, and the situation remains soft. The firmness in Shanghai is due to a lack of supplies from various sources, and prices in production areas are excessively high compared to Shanghai, resulting in very few goods being shipped to Shanghai. Although the price of foreign cotton has fallen compared to the past, it is still not particularly cheap. On Saturday, Shenxin purchased Indian cotton, which was Pingguo coarse lint cotton, in a quantity of 2,000 pieces at a price of 29.5 taels. The cotton market currently still has an upward trend.

Zheng Standard Up 0.04 to 0.05 Taels The opening market was quite strong. There was a lack of sellers in the market. However, because the actual price of cotton was too high, no transactions were made. The total trading volume was 84,200 dan. Dalian Traders Briskly Purchasing Spot Flour 167

丨丨Label Flour Rises Uniformly丨丨

Yesterday's flour market showed a uniform rising trend. Prices for foreign wheat improved by about 0.20 to 0.30 taels. On the trader side, the Tianjin traders remained unchanged, while the Dalian traders showed an intention to buy. The general public was also concerned about the payment of war bonds and deeply worried about significant changes in the gold market, leading to a boost in sentiment. In the afternoon sessions, near-term sentiment showed renewed strength. The Dalian traders continued to push prices up, and spot flour was being drawn out, estimated at 30,000 to 40,000 bags (one source said it was being shipped to northern Manchuria). This situation caused unusual excitement. Futures also showed an upward trend. However, the China Company, which was heavily burdened with new responsibilities, was selling, so the rise was slower. In conclusion, the current month rose by 0.03 taels, January-February rose by 0.025 taels, and March-May rose by 0.015 taels.

Wheat Futures Improve in the Afternoon 168

Yesterday, after the wheat market opened in the morning, the prices for various months were generally stable. There were few transactions and no significant fluctuations. As the afternoon session approached, trading became slightly more active. However, the market prices for various periods were mostly paying attention due to the resurgence of the flour market. This was because the local inventory was depleted, and the market would not be able to move without relief from foreign wheat. Traders with fixed orders would be willing to sell if the market was not good, but would be unwilling to sell if the market was good, so the mentality of hoarding for profit could not be avoided. As a result, the current month improved by 0.03 taels, January remained unchanged, and February, March, and April each rose by 0.03 taels.

Visitor Currency Booms, Then Suddenly Drops by Half a Yuan 169

丨Traders Briskly Purchase After the Fall丨Northern Traders Pay Attention to Visitor Rice丨

Yesterday, there was no market for foreign money. Visitor rice continued to arrive. The amount of visitor currency arriving was booming. There was especially a lot of Du currency from He, and the street was completely stalled. The traders were largely watching. Because the market was sluggish and funds were stranded, the owners had to reluctantly devalue to seek to sell. Thus, the visitor currency suddenly fell by about 0.5 yuan, which allowed the southern traders to buy 1200+ bags of Hunan Wu and ji rice. Other than the southern traders buying visitor currency, there was also a small bit of new Jiangxi machine red rice (200 bags), other sorts are not inquired. The northern traders were, because the Jiangzhe Du gates had not been open, and transport was not viable, so they turned their attention back to visitor rice. 130 bags of Hunan red rice were purchased, priced at 6.75-6.70 yuan. This test run was deemed profitable, and they would continue this going forward. There was Jiangxi machine red rice at 7.70 yuan (200 bags), then there was Chen Yuan rice at 7.60-7.40 yuan (700 bags), Wu machine Yuan rice at 8.089 (214 bags), Hunan machine Yuan rice (200+ bags) at 9.00 yuan.

Comments

The Jinan Demon Bandit Case 182

— Wen Bing

Recently, a rather noteworthy event occurred in society, namely the cracking of the demon bandit case in Jinan. A dispatch from Jinan on the 8th stated:

Early yesterday morning at 7:00 AM, the demon bandit case in Jinan was cracked. The culprits, including Song Wangshi, Le Chuan, Fu Binqi, and others, along with the confiscated full set of imperial paraphernalia, shrines, yellow silk banners, brocade robes, flags, and other items, were escorted to the bureau. The suspects are currently being held in detention. Most notably, according to Li Lechuan's confession, the Xuantong Emperor repeatedly sent people to negotiate, claiming that Japan could supply firearms to help achieve their goals, and that they had practiced numerous spells, so firearms might not be necessary. It is said that Li's conspiracy has been brewing for many years, with so-and-so to be prime minister, and so-and-so to be a general.

After reading this news, we feel there is indeed a need for investigation.

Firstly, it can be said that this was instigated by Japan, or at the very least, by the Japanese puppet state of Manchukuo. Just look at Li Lechuan's confession, "The Xuantong Emperor sent people to say that Japan could supply firearms," and you can get a general idea. Factually speaking, this further proves the possibility of a Japanese conspiracy. Looking back, during the Jinan Incident of the 17th year [of the Republic, 1928], the city was occupied and disturbed by Japanese soldiers for several months, inevitably sowing many seeds of secret conspiracy. After several years of brewing, this has now taken the form of a nascent organization. More recently, since the September 18th Incident [Mukden Incident, 1931], many traitors within the country have been secretly directed by the Japanese, hoping to engage in activities. A major operation by traitors was cracked in Hankou. Even in Shanghai, where people from all over gather, there are probably two such organizations. Moreover, Jinan is an important northern city, with close geographical and political ties to places like Pingjin [Beijing and Tianjin], so the claim of a Japanese conspiracy is indeed credible.

Secondly, the North is originally the cradle of Chinese culture, but in recent times, it has become a haven for feudal remnants and a gathering place for old forces. In the past, the Boxer Rebellion, which triggered the Eight-Nation Alliance invasion, occurred here. Recently, there has been the activity of various occult organizations that chant scriptures and worship Buddhas. This demon bandit organization is just like the Boxers. Moreover, in recent years, natural disasters and man-made calamities have been pressing down on the people. The major conflict between Han and Liu has turned homes into ruins and left people and animals in a state of unrest. Thus, ordinary people, either intoxicated by old novels or poisoned by consistent traditional, old ideas, form fantasies of praying for blessings and creating a "true Son of Heaven." This can also be understood.

In conclusion, the emergence of this demon bandit organization is indeed caused by the terrible current society. Therefore, to eradicate such bandits, it is not enough to simply suppress them. We must first quell the internal strife, clarify the political situation, and resist foreign aggression. Only then will such evils have no opportunity to arise. Otherwise, "the wildfire cannot burn it out, the spring breeze blows and it grows again," and such a farce will just be in full swing.

Common Knowledge

Wine 183

— Sheng Shuigen

Besides being a beverage, wine is also used as an ingredient in cooking in some places (like Shanghai). There are countless names for wine in various countries, but they are all essentially alcohol made from starch. Take starch-rich substances and steam them until cooked, then add yeast. The starch turns into sugar, then add brewing microbes, and the sugar turns into alcohol. The chemical reaction at this time is as follows:

B12H22O11 = H20 + 4C2H6OH4BO2 Maltose Water Alcohol Carbon Dioxide

Method of making wine: Soak glutinous rice in water, then rinse it clean with water. Pour it into a pot and steam it until hot. Take the cooked rice out and spread it on a clean place. After it cools, put it in a jar, add wine yeast, and mix it with the rice. If liquid flows out, add more distiller's yeast and clear water, so that it gradually swells up, becomes very hot, and produces small bubbles. Stir it a dozen times a day, for five or six days. After two or three months, put the cloudy liquid that the rice has turned into in a silk bag and press it on a wine press. That way, you can squeeze out the liquid, which is wine. But we cannot drink this wine yet, because it is raw, so we call it raw wine. After that, after a dozen days, when the wine dregs settle to the bottom of the jar, pour the raw wine into a pot and steam it for twenty minutes, and then this wine can be drunk, because it is cooked. This is roughly the method of making wine.

Types of wine: The types of wine vary due to the amount of alcohol content, the types of raw materials used, and the different additives. Therefore, the wines produced have various names. For example, whiskey contains 44%-55% alcohol, and brandy contains 50%-58% alcohol. Chinese sorghum wine and Fenjiu, etc., contain more than 3-5% alcohol. These are roughly the types of wines we usually drink.

The benefits and harms of wine: Drinking a small amount of wine can invigorate the spirit and activate the muscles and bones, but excessive and indiscriminate drinking is harmful to the kidneys, stomach, nerves, and blood vessels, and can also cause problems for future generations. Most of the mentally deficient and delinquent children in the world are descendants of alcoholics. Drunkenness and madness are also the causes of crime. Therefore, various countries have tried to ban alcohol or impose heavy taxes on it, but without effect. The United States of America, on the surface, has banned it, but there are still many people who secretly make, smuggle, and drink it. Their success in banning alcohol is roughly similar to our China's ban on opium!

Method of sobering up from drunkenness: We should not drink too much of the wine we usually drink. If we drink too much, even those who are good at drinking will easily get drunk. If we get drunk, it often leads to disaster. So now there is a very simple way to sober up a drunk person, roughly speaking: take a bowl of soy sauce soup (must be warm) and give it to the drunk person to drink, and they will immediately become clear-headed as usual. There is also another method: pour wine into a bowl, add preserved eggs and sugar, and even if you drink a lot, you won't get deadly drunk.

Correspondences from Shop Employees

A Small Suggestion 184

Mr. Editor:

In your newspaper on the 5th of this month, I saw the article "The Oppression of the Environment" written by Mr. Xu, which couldn't help but arouse my infinite feelings! Now, which apprentice is not suffering from "the oppression of the environment" and economic difficulties, and had no choice but to abandon their beloved school life and run into this evil society?

Like me, if I had not been affected by the environment in my childhood, without unexpected obstacles, and was able to have a good result, then at least I would have had considerable achievements to comfort myself.

Now, I am standing in the same position as Mr. Xu.

Based on my own experience, under the control of the environment, I live a monotonous life, with no slightest bit of interest, so I am depressed all day long. I think most apprentices must feel the same boredom. So, if we want to break this boredom, we must unite. The following is my small suggestion:

First step, for all apprentices who communicate in the [blank] column, I hope that the teacher will introduce us, so that we can be free. If this allows people with similar personalities to gradually become familiar with each other, then feelings can be melted together.

Second step, after feelings are melted together, we can further become close friends. Then, in the future, in terms of career, we can help each other. That is, in terms of life improvement and academic cultivation, it is also very beneficial.

The above is my humble opinion, I wonder what Mr. Xu thinks of it? At the same time, I hope that the apprentices in this city will put forward their opinions for discussion. As for the specific method, it is necessary to ask the enthusiastic teacher to stand in a leading position and indicate to us a direction to proceed. Hong Mingchang 12.8.

Editor's note: Under the same lifestyle, the joys and sorrows suffered are mostly the same.

Therefore, since Mr. Xu Jue's letter "The Oppression of the Environment" was published, we have received many similar letters one after another! Bu Chang said that his salary is limited and insufficient to support the family, that he is living the life of a horse all day long without the opportunity to read books and newspapers: not that since his father died, he has been unable to repay a large amount of debt, but that his mother is old and his sister is young, and he sees that there is no money to pay for the funeral and marriage, etc. ...... It's simply endless. In short, it is nothing more than because of the misery of life and economic panic, that they want to find a way out.

These letters, when we read them, are enough to seal and shed tears丨express deep sympathy. We want to try our best to find a way to solve these difficult problems, blowing everyone's cloud, so that everyone's life can be satisfied; but, what method do we have? We must know that everything in society is closely related. In this time of internal and external troubles, in this environment of sluggish market and rural bankruptcy; we can say: The problems of you are not individual, but social, nor are they individual incompetence, but the fundamental defects of the current society. Unless this defect is corrected and transformed, the individual's problems can never be solved.

We must also know that purely "looking up at the roof and sighing" is useless; sighing is sighing, and pain is still pain, right? The god of sorrow will not be as timid as a swallow, and be frightened away by your sigh, if you do not immediately think of an effective way to drive it away, it will often come to visit you. But where is the effective method? It is not in "the edge of the sky, the corner of the sea," it is still in each person's own self. The first to be able to see this and break the air of misery and sorrow, is to push Hongjun's letter!

Although the method mentioned in Hongjun's letter is still the principle of the preliminary stage, it is very valuable for public discussion. In the amateur talk of the second issue of the amateur weekly this Sunday (11th), the reporter has already briefly mentioned it, and now it will be published below, hoping that friends will concentrate their efforts and express their great opinions on this goal.

Novel

Writing a Letter to a Friend's Wife (Continuation 5) 186

— Qin Shouou

"Why does your stomach hurt a bit!:::" It hurts so badly! When landing at Donggou, because I had already heard the Great Classics issue three orders and five applications to restrict you from going into the water when you arrived at the bathhouse, I deliberately hummed about a stomach ache, and as a result, of course, everyone else went into the water together, but I got the good job of accompanying you.

"Let's go over there and have a few ice creams!" I was so happy that I seemed to have suddenly reduced my age by ten years. Taking your arm, which was white, tender, and smooth, like a sculpture made of ivory, we laughed and jumped all the way to a frozen-drink shop built with bamboo poles and reed mats.

"That's right! You should drink more ice cream when your stomach hurts!" In your bright and lively eyes, as beautiful as the stars in the sky, a kind of smile that was half joy and half teasing flickered at me. I myself couldn't help but laugh out loud.

Little friend! Little piggy! Brother! 丨You are a man, not a woman. 丨You are really the most beautiful and intelligent little elf in the world! I will always admire you.

I myself admit that my emotional impulses are indeed a bit excessive: often when I am frustrated or proud, I have many abnormal actions. That day, of course, I was very proud, so cup after cup of Beauty Brand ice cream went into my stomach as easily as a mouthful of clear water. In an instant, it was already the beginning of the sixth cup.

"Don't drink anymore!" You reached out and snatched it away.

"Okay! Just this one cup, let me drink it again!" I pestered his mother like a naughty child. At the same time, I actually opened up five fingers, preparing to implement a forcible seizure policy.

Although there were extremely sincere smiles floating on our faces, neither of us was willing to give up our own opinions: a cup of ice cream became the target of the two sides' contention. In the end, you saw that you couldn't resist me: unexpectedly, the clever you actually threw this target in one hand to the ground, and at the same time stretched out your toes, and solved everything with just one kick.

You were obviously victorious, and lay on my knees laughing like crazy.

"They are so intimate!" The people on the side seat were quietly issuing a kind of envious whisper.

"They:::what are they?" I asked, leaning over your ear.

"They are probably brothers and sisters!" You replied vaguely.

"No! Mostly cousins!" I teased very proudly.

Haha! Dear little friend! Look, I remember this thing so carefully! To be honest, as long as everything that happened when you and I were together is engraved on my brain nerves like a branding iron.

Even the most common and simplest little action will never be missed.

In Gaoqiao, I drank ice cream wildly because of the excitement of being proud, and in Avenue Joffre, I drank ice cream wildly because of the excitement of being frustrated. Although it was the same excitement, but when I was in Zhonggaoqiao, you were limiting me by my side, so it wasn't excessive; on this day, those Russian girls next to me were urging me for the sake of their business, and there was no reason to come and dissuade me again! So, within fifty minutes, I actually finished drinking, no, I simply swallowed five large cups of ice cream. In the end, I added two large cups of red bean shaved ice. It can be said that I have done my best to drink water!

However, people are not made of iron after all! Half a day's work of wind and rain, and a large amount of cold drinks, finally broke out together when I lay in bed. Vomiting, diarrhea, and fever all came to shake hands with me at the same time. The next day, 丨was the morning of the day I got up·The sunlight slowly stretched out its head from the window, and sent me a mocking sneer through the glass: I got a headache and struggled desperately. My head hurt like Sun Wukong heard the Tightening Spell, it hurt so much that it seemed to have split into several pieces.

"Ah! I really can't leave today!" I reluctantly climbed out of bed, but unexpectedly, my body seemed to be stuffed into a bag of cotton, shaking and unable to stand straight; my legs were also determined not to obey my orders anymore, and walking one step was simply more difficult than climbing a mountain. Therefore, I had a half-negative thought of starting a day later. (To be continued)

Film Supplement

Strange Overseas News: Animals and Insects Can Also Perform 187

— Lin

Movies are realistic everywhere, so everything in the universe that people can see should also be seen in movies, so rare birds and animals, poisonous snakes and insects, etc., can also be seen in movies from time to time to expand our people's horizons. Among the various film companies in Hollywood, the one that needs the most various animals is Paramount. And Mr. Bill Pierce, the director of the purchasing department of Paramount, also has quite a wide range of talent, so the company, no matter what it needs, he can always find a way to get it, and never fails to live up to his mission. Not long ago, this Mr. Bill Pierce received an order from the company, telling him to find two thousand Crimson formicidae. Of course, Crimson is red, but what is formicidae? Bill had never heard of it, so he turned to the foreign Kangxi dictionary, and it turned out that it was the scientific name of a kind of red ant. What are these red ants used for? They are used in the movie "King of the Beasts". There is a scene in which two hunters are killed by a lion, but red ants gather and join the bodies of the two people, and are finished in an instant. So Bill searched for the gathering place of this terrifying red ant in southern California. By chance, a gentleman discovered this red ant in his garden and wanted to find a way to exterminate it. So Bill discussed it with him, using honey to lure the red ants, put them in cans, and took them to the film scene for application.

Bill feels that there is no difficulty in finding and training various kinds of beasts, but ordinary training is absolutely different from that under the thousands of strong lights in the photography studio. Often, an animal, after a long period of training, becomes as dull as a wooden chicken when it arrives at the photography studio, or even reveals its violent nature due to fright. Furthermore, fierce beasts such as lions and tigers only recognize the people who train them, and do not buy anyone else's account at all. Once, Paramount was filming a scene in a circus. A lion filmed a scene all morning, and it was really as tame as a cat rabbit. When the trainer was present, all the actors mixed with it without any fear. When it was time for lunch, the trainer went to eat. The lion's cage was placed in the photography studio. Several actors, because they had been playing with it all morning, thought it was very kind, and still went near the cage to tease the lion. Who knew that when the lion saw that the trainer was not around, it pounced on the people who entered the cage, and two were knocked to the ground by the lion at the same time. Fortunately, the trainer arrived in time and saved the lives of the two people, but that danger was really imminent.

Rochelle Hudson's charm is famous, and she is always willing to show off her jade arms. Her slim figure is really something that no one can not praise. She was born in Oklahoma eighteen years ago, and became famous as soon as she arrived in Hollywood, which is surprising to many people who cannot reach her. We recently screened "Fanny Foley" in Nanjing.

Reader's Opinions

The Material of the Film 189

— Xue Fan

We feel that although the number of films published recently is very large, their descriptive vision is too biased on one side. Human affairs are so complex and life is so changing, is it possible that the material of the script can only be turned around and only between these men and women? What we see in the movie theater is just love stories, and we are really tired of watching them! We also understand that the producer's vision is biased towards love, in order to cater to the general audience, so no matter whether the story of the film is logical or not, and no matter whether the equipment of the film is sound or not, as long as there are men and women in the film, talking about love, it is hastily premiered. Of course, this kind of film can also be welcomed by a part of the people, but this aspect of success is the failure of the film itself!"

I am not absolutely opposed to the film not telling love stories. What I mean is: besides love stories, there are many fragments of life that can be described, and there are many satirizing, tragic aspects of life that can be used as film materials. If the director's vision can shine around him, where is there no good material? If the vision can reach the lower class, then its achievements are even unlimited! Let's look at the current large number of domestic films. Which film that talks about love and describes love is worth praising? And only one "Humanity" is more successful. In short, it seems that the current Chinese society does not need the sound of [] and paper fans, but needs a kind of how to stimulate this dying nation and make a new life for a nation? Wise screenwriters! I wonder what you think?

Celebrity Anecdotes

Ramon Novarro's Rise to Fame (Part 2) 190

— Xi Meng

He mingled in the romantic art world for a few years, and then went from New York to Los Angeles (where Hollywood is located). He left Marlene Muugen's song and dance troupe to seek the realization of his dream of one thousand dollars a week. At that time, his compatriot Valentino had already become famous, and people in the entire American film industry worshiped him like an idol. But Ramon Novarro continued his work without any regrets, and was quite content with himself.

What made Valentino famous was Rex Ingram. At that time, Ingram was engaged in the filming of The Prisoner of Zenda, and the role of Rupert of Hentzau had not yet been found. Ramon had already acted in a film at that time, but his experience was not very rich. He got a letter of introduction from a friend and went to see Ingram.

Ingram glanced at him and shook his head. He said, "I'm very sorry, your appearance happens to be the opposite of my character Rupert. Rupert is very tall, has fair skin, a haughty attitude, and is older than you." At that time, Ramon was only twenty-two years old, with black eyes and black hair, and was completely representative of Mexicans.

Ramon failed for a while, but he asked Ingram to let him try it anyway. Ingram told him that he could come again tomorrow, but he must not have any extravagant hopes, because his chances were as difficult as ascending to heaven. Ramon also asked Ingram to tell him what the character's character and appearance were like. Ingram wrote many words on the back of his letter of introduction and gave it to Ramon, telling him to go back.

Ramon seemed very disappointed to take back his letter of introduction and walked home, carefully studying the character's identity and appearance. He suddenly jumped up, ran to a clothing store, selected a set of clothes, and ran to Ingram's place early the next morning. When Ingram looked up, he was so surprised that he opened his mouth and couldn't speak. It turned out that Ramon's appearance had been changed to be exactly like the ideal character. Later, Ingram looked at him carefully again, and put a monocle on him. Ramon Novarro's face was still very smooth at that time, and the monocle slid down when he put it on, but the role of Rupert of Hentzau belonged to Ramon Novarro. This is the beginning of his rise to become a big star. (End)

Anecdotes and Scandals

A Scene of Ma Loufen and Li Minghui 191

— Zheng Lixuan

When Ma Loufen was thirteen years old, she was studying at Wanzhu Primary School in the Nine Acres area within the city. At that time, it so happened that the younger sister of the Li family, admiring the reputation of Wanzhu, disguised herself as a boy and came to study there. Her class was the same as Ma's; coincidentally, she also shared a desk with Ma. At first, of course, no one knew that a girl had suddenly appeared in the pure primary school. However, as time went on, Miss Li's behavior inevitably revealed her true identity. Moreover, because she was beautiful and charming, several classmates became particularly close to her. As for Ma Loufen, naturally, "being near the water tower, one gets the moon first." The two of them were almost inseparable at school. Whenever there was a holiday, Ma often rented a bicycle, letting Miss Li sit behind her, and they would ride to quiet places in the suburbs to play. At that time, their intimate demeanor certainly aroused jealousy among all the classmates. After two semesters, they attracted too much public attention, so they transferred to another school together. However, their affection remained strong. Later, Miss Li joined the singing and dancing world, and Ma also followed her. However, Miss Li's fame became too great, causing Ma to feel that she could never catch up. Nevertheless, Miss Li never forgot their past friendship. Thus, with the encouragement and support of Miss Li and her father, Jinhui, Ma Loufen achieved her current status.

— Xing Su

When Xue Juexian met Wang Cilong in Hong Kong, he asked Wang to introduce talent to assist in film production in Shanghai. Wang introduced his old friend, But Du Yu. Now that Xue has come to Shanghai and contacted But Du Yu, But has agreed to assist in the preparations. In the future, matters such as directing, set design, and hiring actors will all be entrusted to But. Whether the film production work will be entrusted to the American company Johnson is yet to be decided. Zhou Shilu will be in charge of the photography. The first work currently being prepared for filming is the sound film "White Gold Dragon," a masterpiece originally performed by Xue on stage. The script is from a foreign play, and the original text of the foreign script is given to But Du Yu as a reference when directing.

The Experience of Reading a Synopsis 193

— Chaoyang

Every theater has a synopsis. Its responsibility is to tell you the plot of the movie. In my experience, it's best not to read the synopsis before the movie starts.

The reason is this: If you've read the synopsis, you'll know the plot in advance, and the movie won't arouse much interest in you. If a woman is loved by two men, it's so boring if we already know which man will win! Knowing the plot in advance, your spirit will relax, and you won't be tense at all.

Movie Essays

The Habit of Freely Squeezing Tears 194

— Chen Dabe

The most difficult things to distinguish between crying and laughing are our eyes. The reason why a crying expression can often resemble a laughing one is because the eyes are too focused. When a person laughs, their spirit is active, so their eyes are focused; when crying, their spirit is passive, so their eyes are scattered. Without the help of a single tear, if you try to leave a crying expression for the camera, the result will often look like laughter. This is because the eyes are too focused.

When shooting crying close-ups (Close-in) on a large set, except for a few stars who have already developed the habit of freely squeezing tears, usually glycerin is dripped into the actor's eye sockets to replace real tears. Two tears slowly flowing down the face can completely conceal all the weaknesses of a crying expression. From this, it can be seen how valuable tears are in a crying expression.

Although the method of using glycerin is very clever, the taste when it is dripped into the eye sockets is similar to that of eye drops given by a doctor to patients with eye diseases. After dripping in glycerin, you still have to close your eyelids and wait for the lighting and camera to be fully adjusted, and then force out those two drops of glycerin when the camera starts rolling. It always looks a little unnatural.

For this reason, we should "aim high" when practicing and develop this habit of freely squeezing tears as early as possible. In the eyes of inexperienced people, it may be thought that this is impossible. In fact, as long as you are willing to put in a little effort in both psychology and breathing, freely squeezing tears is not a difficult task.

(The "Ugly and Unbearable Expressions" published yesterday should have been placed before the "Crying Without Breathing Assistance" from the day before yesterday. Due to the author's forgetting to indicate the number, this error occurred. Please forgive the readers. Author's note)
